sutaḥ sṛñjayasya abhavat putraḥ vīraḥ rājā puraṃjayaḥ deveṣu sa parijñātaḥ pratiṣṭhita yaśāḥ tathā mahāmanāḥ nāma sutaḥ mahāsālasya dhārmikaḥ jajñe vīraḥ sura gaṇaiḥ pūjitaḥ sa mahāmanāḥ uśīnaram ca dharma jñam titikṣum ca mahā balam uśīnarasya patnyaḥ tu pañca rājarṣi vaṃśa jāḥ nṛgā kṛmī navā darvā pañcamā ca dṛṣadvatī uśīnarasya putrāḥ tu pañca tāsu kula udvahāḥ tapasā ca eva mahatā jātāḥ vṛddhasya ca ātmajāḥ nṛgāyāḥ tu nṛgaḥ putraḥ kṛmyāḥ kṛmiḥ ajāyata navāyāḥ tu navaḥ putraḥ darvāyāḥ suvrataḥ abhavat dṛṣadvatyāḥ tu saṃjajñe śibiḥ auśīnaraḥ nṛpa navasya navarāṣṭram tu kṛmeḥ tu kṛmilā purī suvratasya tathā ambaṣṭhā titikṣoḥ tu prajāḥ śṛṇu titikṣuḥ abhavat rājā pūrvasyām diśi bhārata phenāt tu sutapāḥ jajñe jajñe sutapasaḥ sutaḥ baliḥ mānuṣa yonau tu sa rājā kāñcaneṣudhiḥ mahā yogī sa tu baliḥ babhūva nṛpatiḥ purā putrān utpādayām āsa pañca vaṃśa karān bhuvi puṇḍraḥ kaliṅgaḥ ca tathā bāleyam kṣatram ucyate bāleyāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ ca eva tasya vaṃśa karāḥ bhuvi mahā yogi tvam āyuḥ ca kalpasya parimāṇāt caturaḥ niyatān varṇān tvam ca sthāpayitā iti ha iti uktaḥ vibhunā rājā baliḥ śāntim parām yayau kālena mahatā rājan svam ca sthānam upāgamat teṣām janapadāḥ pañca vaṅga aṅgāḥ suhmakāḥ tathā kaliṅgāḥ puṇḍrakāḥ ca eva prajāḥ tu aṅgasya mama śṛṇu aṅga putraḥ mahān āsīt rāja indraḥ dadhivāhanaḥ yajatā saha śakreṇa somaḥ pītaḥ mahātmanā lomapādaḥ iti khyātaḥ yasya śāntā sutā bhavat tasya dāśarathiḥ vīraḥ caturaṅgaḥ mahā yaśāḥ ṛṣyaśṛṅga prabhāvena jajñe kula vivardhanaḥ caturaṅgasya putraḥ tu pṛthulākṣaḥ iti smṛtaḥ pṛthulākṣa sutaḥ rājā campaḥ nāma mahā yaśāḥ campasya tu purī campā yā pūrvam mālinī babhau tatas vibhāṇḍakaḥ tasya vāraṇam śatru vāraṇam avatārayām āsa mahīm mantraiḥ vāhanam uttamam tasya putra śatam tu āsīt aṅgānām kula vardhanam ete aṅga vaṃśa jāḥ sarve rājānaḥ kīrtitāḥ mayā satya vratāḥ mahātmānaḥ prajāvantaḥ mahā rathāḥ śṛṇu vaṃśam anuproktam yatra jātaḥ asi pārthiva rājan matināraḥ mahīpatiḥ matināra sutāḥ ca āsan trayaḥ parama dhārmikāḥ sarve veda vrata snātāḥ brahmaṇyāḥ satya vādinaḥ taṃsoḥ suraughaḥ rājarṣiḥ dharmanetraḥ mahā yaśāḥ brahma vādī parākrāntaḥ tasya bhāryā upadānavī duḥṣantam atha suḥṣantam pravīram anagham tathā duḥṣantasya tu dāyādaḥ bharataḥ nāma vīryavān cakravartī sutaḥ jajñe duḥṣantasya mahā yaśāḥ śakuntalāyām bharataḥ yasya nāmnā stha bhāratāḥ bharatasya vinaṣṭeṣu tanayeṣu mahīpateḥ mātṝṇām tāta kopeṇa yathā te kathitam tadā bṛhaspateḥ aṅgirasaḥ putraḥ rājan mahā muniḥ sa ca api vitathaḥ putrān janayām āsa pañca vai kāśikaḥ ca mahāsattvaḥ tathā gṛtsamatiḥ prabhuḥ tathā gṛtsamateḥ putrāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ viśaḥ kāśyasya kāśayaḥ rājan putraḥ dīrghatapāḥ tathā athā ketumantaḥ putraḥ vīraḥ bhīmarathaḥ smṛtaḥ divodāsaḥ iti khyātaḥ sarva rakṣaḥ praṇāśanaḥ etasmin eva kāle tu purīm vārāṇasīm nṛpaḥ śūnyām niveśayām āsa kṣemakaḥ nāma rākṣasaḥ śaptā hi sā matimatā nikumbhena mahātmanā śūnyā varṣa sahasram vai bhavitrī iti nara ṛṣabha tasyām tu śapta mātrāyām divodāsaḥ prajeśvaraḥ saṃnyaveśayat bhadraśreṇyasya putrāṇām śatam uttama dhanvinām hatvā niveśayām āsa divodāsaḥ prajeśvaraḥ alarkaḥ rāja putraḥ ca rājā saṃnatimant bhuvi hehayasya tu dāyādyam hṛtavan vai mahīpatiḥ ājahre pitṛ dāyādyam divodāsa hṛtam balāt divodāsena bālaḥ hi ghṛṇayā sa visarjitaḥ aṣṭārathaḥ nāma nṛpaḥ sutaḥ bhīmarathasya vai tena putreṣu bāleṣu prahṛtam tasya bhārata vairasya antam mahā rāja kṣatriyeṇa vidhitsatā alarkaḥ kāśi rājaḥ tu brahmaṇyaḥ satya saṃgaraḥ ṣaṣṭim varṣa sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭim varṣa śatāni ca yuvā rūpeṇa saṃpannaḥ āsīt kāśi kula udvahaḥ lopāmudrā prasādena parama āyuḥ avāpa saḥ vayasaḥ ante mahā bāhuḥ hatvā kṣemaka rākṣasam ramyām niveśayām āsa purīm vārāṇasīm nṛpaḥ alarkasya tu dāyādaḥ kṣemaḥ nāma mahā yaśāḥ varṣaketoḥ tu dāyādaḥ vibhuḥ nāma prajeśvaraḥ sutaḥ abhavat mahā tejāḥ rājā parama dhārmikaḥ ete tu aṅgirasaḥ putrāḥ jātāḥ vaṃśe atha bhārgave brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca bharata ṛṣabha ajamīḍhaḥ dvimīḍhaḥ ca purumīḍhaḥ ca vīryavān ajamīḍhasya patnyaḥ tu tisraḥ vai yaśasā anvitāḥ nīlī ca keśinī ca eva dhūminī ca vara aṅganā ajamīḍhasya keśinyām jajñe jahnuḥ pratāpavān na icchataḥ plāvayām āsa tasya gaṅgā ca tat sadaḥ tayā ca plāvitam dṛṣṭvā yajñavāṭam samantataḥ eṣa te triṣu lokeṣu saṃkṣipya apaḥ pibāmi aham tatas pītām mahātmānaḥ gaṅgām dṛṣṭvā mahā ṛṣayaḥ upaninyuḥ mahābhāgām duhitṛ tvāya jāhnavīm yuvanāśvasya putrīm tu kāverīm jahnuḥ āvahat ajakasya tu dāyādaḥ balākāśvaḥ mahīpatiḥ babhūva mṛgayā śīlaḥ kuśikaḥ tasya ca ātmajaḥ pahlavaiḥ saha saṃvṛddhaḥ rājā vana caraiḥ sa ha viśvāmitraḥ tu gādheyaḥ rājā viśvarathaḥ ca ha viśvajit viśvakṛt ca eva tathā satyavatī nṛpa viśvāmitrasya tu sutāḥ devarāta ādayaḥ smṛtāḥ prakhyātāḥ triṣu lokeṣu teṣām nāmāni me śṛṇu devaśravāḥ katiḥ ca eva yasmāt kātyāyanāḥ smṛtāḥ śālā patiḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ reṇuḥ yasya atha reṇukā sāṃkṛtyaḥ gālavaḥ rājan maudgalyaśva iti viśrutāḥ teṣām khyātāni gotrāṇi kauśikānām mahātmanām pārthivāḥ devarātāḥ ca sālaṅkāyana sauśravāḥ lohityāḥ yamadūtaḥ ca tathā kārīṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ viśrutāḥ kauśikāḥ rājan tathā anye saindhavāyanāḥ ṛṣi antara vivāhyāḥ ca kauśikāḥ bahavaḥ smṛtāḥ viśvāmitra ātmajānām tu śunaḥśepaḥ agrajaḥ smṛtaḥ bhārgavaḥ kauśika tvam hi prāptaḥ sa muni sattamaḥ śabara ādayaḥ ca sapta anye viśvāmitrasya vai sutāḥ dṛṣadvatī sutaḥ ca api viśvāmitrāt atha aṣṭakaḥ ājamīḍhaḥ aparaḥ vaṃśaḥ śrūyatām bharata ṛṣabhaiḥ ajamīḍhāt tu nīlyām vai suśāntiḥ udapadyata purujātiḥ suśānteḥ tu bāhyāśvaḥ purujāteḥ bāhyāśva tanayāḥ pañca babhūvuḥ amara upamāḥ mudgalaḥ sṛñjayaḥ ca eva rājā bṛhadiṣuḥ tathā yavīnaraḥ ca vikrāntaḥ kṛmilāśvaḥ ca pañcamaḥ pañca ime rakṣaṇāya alam deśānām iti viśrutāḥ pañcānām viddhi pāñcālān sphītān puṇyajana āvṛtān alam saṃrakṣaṇe teṣām pāñcālāḥ iti viśrutāḥ mudgalasya tu dāyādaḥ maudgalyaḥ su mahā yaśāḥ āsīt pañcavanaḥ putraḥ sṛñjayasya mahātmanaḥ somadattasya dāyādaḥ sahadevaḥ mahā yaśāḥ teṣām yavīyāḥ pṛṣataḥ drupadasya pitā prabhuḥ mahiṣī tu ajamīḍhasya dhūminī putra gṛddhinī tṛtīyā tava pūrveṣām jananī pṛthivīpate sā tu putra arthinī devī vrata caryā samāhitā tapaḥ varṣā śatam tepe strībhiḥ parama duścaram dhūminyā sa tayā devyā ajamīḍhaḥ sameyivān ṛkṣam sā janayām āsa dhūma varṇam sudarśanam ṛkṣāt saṃvaraṇaḥ jajñe kuruḥ saṃvaraṇāt tathā yaḥ prayāgāt apakramya kurukṣetram cakāra ha puṇyam ca ramaṇīyam ca puṇya kṛdbhiḥ niṣevitam tasya anvavāyaḥ su mahān yasya nāmnā stha kauravāḥ kuroḥ ca putrāḥ catvāraḥ sudhanvā sudhanuḥ tathā parīkṣit ca mahā bāhuḥ pravaraḥ ca arimejayaḥ vidūrathasya dāyādaḥ ṛkṣaḥ eva mahā rathaḥ dvitīyaḥ sa babhau rājā nāmnā tena eva saṃjñitaḥ dvau ṛkṣau tava vaṃśe asmin dvau eva ca parīkṣitau pratīpaḥ bhīmasenasya pratīpasya tu śāṃtanuḥ devāpiḥ bāhlikaḥ ca eva trayaḥ eva mahā rathāḥ śāṃtanoḥ prasavaḥ tu eṣa yatra jātaḥ asi pārthiva bāhlikasya tu rājyam vai saptabāhlyam viśām pate bāhlikasya sutaḥ ca eva somadattaḥ mahā yaśāḥ jajñire somadattāt tu bhūriḥ bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ upādhyāyaḥ tu devānām devāpiḥ abhavat muniḥ cyavanasya putraḥ kṛtakaḥ iṣṭaḥ ca āsīt mahātmanaḥ śāṃtanuḥ tu abhavat rājā kauravāṇām dhuraṃdharaḥ kālī vicitravīryam tu janayām āsa bhārata śāṃtanoḥ dayitam putram dharma ātmānam akalmaṣam dhṛtarāṣṭram ca pāṇḍum ca viduram ca api ajījanat pāṇḍoḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ putraḥ saubhadraḥ tasya ca ātmajaḥ gobhānoḥ tu sutaḥ rājā triśānuḥ aparājitaḥ anapatyaḥ abhavat rājā yajvā vipula dakṣiṇaḥ duhitā saṃmatā nāma tasya āsīt pṛthivīpateḥ dakṣiṇā artham hi sā dattā saṃvartāya mahātmane evam yayāteḥ śāpena jarā saṃkramaṇe tadā pauravam turvasoḥ vaṃśaḥ praviveśa nṛpa uttama duḥṣantasya tu dāyādaḥ śarutthāmaḥ prajeśvaraḥ śarutthāmāt atha ākrīḍaḥ catvāraḥ tasya ca ātmajāḥ pāṇḍyaḥ ca keralaḥ ca eva kolaḥ colaḥ ca pārthivaḥ teṣām janapadāḥ sphītāḥ pāṇḍyaḥ colaḥ ca keralāḥ yuddham su mahat āsīt hi māsān pari caturdaśa aṅgārasya tu dāyādaḥ gāndhāraḥ nāma pārthivaḥ khyāyate yasya nāmnā vai gāndhāra viṣayaḥ mahān gāndhāra deśa jāḥ ca eva turagāḥ vājinām varāḥ dhṛtāt tu duduhaḥ jajñe pracetāḥ tasya ca ātmajaḥ babhūvuḥ tu yadoḥ putrāḥ pañca deva suta upamāḥ sahasradaḥ payodaḥ ca kroṣṭā nīlaḥ añjikaḥ tathā sahasradasya dāyādāḥ trayaḥ parama dhārmikāḥ kṛtavīryaḥ kṛtaujāḥ ca kṛtadhanvā tathā eva ca kṛtāgniḥ ca caturthaḥ abhūt kṛtavīryāt tathā arjunaḥ sa hi varṣa śatam taptvā tapaḥ parama duścaram tam ārādhayām āsa kārtavīryaḥ atri sambhavam pūrvam bāhu sahasram tu prārthitam paramam varam ugreṇa pṛthivīm jitvā dharmeṇa eva anurañjanam saṃgrāmān su bahūn jitvā hatvā ca arīn sahasraśas saṃgrāme vartamānasya vadham ca abhyadhikāt raṇe yogāt yogeśvarasya agre prādurbhavati māyayā tena iyam pṛthivī kṛtsnā saptadvīpā sa pattanā prāptāni vidhinā rājñā śrūyante janamejaya sarve yajñāḥ mahā bāho tasya āsan bhūri dakṣiṇāḥ sarve kāñcana yūpāḥ ca sarve kāñcana vedayaḥ sarve devaiḥ mahā rāja vimāna sthaiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ varīdāsa ātmajaḥ vidvāḥ mahimnā tasya vismitaḥ na nūnam kārtavīryasya gatim yāsyanti pārthivāḥ sa hi saptasu dvīpeṣu khaḍgī carmī śarāsanī rathī dvīpān anucaran yogī saṃdṛśyate nṛbhiḥ sa bhikṣām adadāt vīraḥ sapta dvīpān vibhāvasoḥ arjunaḥ nāma kauravyaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ kunti nandanaḥ tapasvī brāhmaṇaḥ ca tvām haniṣyati sa bhārgavaḥ a naṣṭa dravya tā yasya babhūva amitra karśana rāmāt tatas asya mṛtyuḥ vai tasya śāpāt mahā muneḥ tasya putra śatasya āsan pañca śeṣāḥ mahātmanaḥ kṛtāstrāḥ balinaḥ śūrāḥ dharma ātmānaḥ yaśasvinaḥ śūrasenaḥ ca śūraḥ ca dhṛṣṭoktaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ eva ca jayadhvajaḥ ca nāmnā āsīt āvantyaḥ nṛpatiḥ mahān kārtavīryasya tanayāḥ vīryavantaḥ mahā rathāḥ tasya putrāḥ śata ākhyāḥ tu tālajaṅghāḥ iti śrutāḥ teṣām kule mahā rāja hehayānām mahātmanām vītihotrāḥ sujātāḥ ca bhojāḥ ca avantayaḥ tathā tauṇḍikerāḥ iti khyātāḥ tālajaṅghāḥ tathā eva ca bharatāḥ ca sujātāḥ ca bahu tvāt na anukīrtitāḥ madhoḥ putra śatam tu āsīt vṛṣaṇaḥ tasya vaṃśa bhāj tu yādavāḥ yadunā ca agre nirucyante ca hehayāḥ na tasya vitta nāśaḥ syāt naṣṭam pratilabhet ca saḥ ete yayāti putrāṇām pañca vaṃśāḥ viśām pate ye lokān dhārayanti vai bhūtāni iva mahā rāja pañca sthāvara jaṅgamam śrutvā pañca visargam tu rājā dharma artha kovidaḥ vaśī bhavati pañcānām ātmajānām tathā īśvaraḥ labhet pañca varān ca eṣa durlabhān iha laukikān āyuḥ kīrtim dhanam putrān aiśvaryam bhūyaḥ eva ca dhāraṇāt śravaṇāt ca eva pañcavargasya bhārata kroṣṭoḥ tu śṛṇu rāja indra vaṃśam uttama pūruṣam kroṣṭoḥ hi vaṃśam śrutvā imam sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate yasya anvavāya jaḥ viṣṇuḥ hariḥ vṛṣṇi kula prabhuḥ uvāca gāndhārī ca eva mādrī ca kroṣṭoḥ bhārye babhūvatuḥ gāndhārī janayām āsa anamitram mahā balam mādrī yudhājitam putram tatas vai devamīḍhuṣam teṣām vaṃśaḥ tridhā bhūtaḥ vṛṣṇīnām kula vardhanaḥ mādryāḥ putrau tu jajñāte śrutau vṛṣṇi andhakau ubhau jajñāte tanayau vṛṣṇeḥ śvaphalkaḥ citrakaḥ tathā trīṇi varṣāṇi viṣaye na avarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ sa tatra vāsayām āsa śvaphalkam parama arcitam śvaphalkaḥ kāśi rājasya sutām bhāryām avindata gāndinīm nāma sā gām tu dadau vipreṣu nityaśas dātā yajvā ca dhīraḥ ca śrutavān atithi priyaḥ akrūraḥ suṣuve tasmāt śvaphalkāt bhūri dakṣiṇaḥ māvāha prativāhau ca sundarā ca vara aṅganā akrūreṇa augrasenyām tu su gātrāyām kuru nandana aśvagrīvaḥ aśvabāhuḥ ca supārśvaka gaveṣaṇau ariṣṭanemiḥ aśvaḥ ca sudharmā dharmabhṛt tathā subāhuḥ bahubāhuḥ ca śraviṣṭhā śravaṇe striyau aśmakyām janayām āsa śūram vai devamīḍhuṣam mahiṣyām jajñire śūrāt bhojyāyām puruṣāḥ daśa mahābāhuḥ pūrvam ānakadundubhiḥ mahān abhavat divi papāta puṣpa varṣam ca śūrasya bhavane mahat yasya āsīt puruṣa agryasya kāntiḥ candramasaḥ yathā devabhāgaḥ tatas jajñe tatas devaśravāḥ punar anādhṛṣṭiḥ kanavakaḥ vatsavant atha gṛñjimaḥ śyāmaḥ śamīkaḥ gaṇḍūṣaḥ pañca ca asya vara aṅganāḥ pṛthukīrtiḥ pṛthā ca eva śrutadevā śrutaśravāḥ rājādhidevī ca tathā pañca etāḥ vīra mātaraḥ kuntyasya śrutadevāyām agṛdhnuḥ suṣuve nṛpaḥ śrutaśravāyām caidyaḥ tu śiśupālaḥ mahā balaḥ pṛthukīrtyām tu saṃjajñe tanayaḥ vṛddhaśarmaṇaḥ karūṣa adhipateḥ vīraḥ dantavaktraḥ mahā balaḥ pṛthām duhitaram cakre kauntyaḥ tām pāṇḍuḥ āvahat yasyām sa dharma vid rājā dharmāt jajñe yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhīmasenaḥ tathā vātāt indrāt ca eva dhanaṃjayaḥ anamitrāt śaniḥ jajñe kaniṣṭhāt vṛṣṇi nandanāt paṇḍitānām param prāhuḥ devaśravasam uddhavam aśmakī alabhata apatnyam anādhṛṣṭim yaśasvinam nivṛtta śatrum śatrughnam śrutadevā vyajāyata śrutadevā prajātaḥ tu naiṣādaḥ yaḥ pariśrutaḥ ekalavyaḥ mahā rāja niṣādaiḥ parivardhitaḥ gaṇḍūṣāya tu aputrāya viṣvaksenaḥ dadau sutam cārudeṣṇam sucārum ca pañcālam kṛtalakṣaṇam a saṃgrāmeṇa yaḥ vīraḥ na avartata kadā cana raukmiṇeyaḥ mahā bāhuḥ kanīyāḥ bharata ṛṣabha vāyasānām sahasrāṇi yam yāntam pṛṣṭhatas anvayuḥ cārūn adya upayokṣyāmaḥ cārudeṣṇa hatān iti vīraḥ ca aśvahanuḥ ca eva vīrau tau atha gṛñjimau śyāma putraḥ sumitraḥ tu śamīkaḥ rājyam āvahat ajātaśatruḥ śatrūṇām jajñe tasya vināśanaḥ vasudevasya tu sutān kīrtayiṣyāmi tān śṛṇu vṛṣṇeḥ trividham etam tu bahu śākham mahā ojasam uvāca pauravī rohiṇī nāma bāhlikasya ātmajā nṛpa jyeṣṭhā patnī mahā rāja dayitā ānakadundubheḥ lebhe jyeṣṭham sutam rāmam śāraṇam śaṭham eva ca durdamam damanam śvabhram piṇḍāraka kuśīnarau citrām nāma kumārīm ca rohiṇī tanayāḥ nava vasudevāt ca devakyām jajñe śauriḥ mahā yaśāḥ rāmāt ca niśaṭhaḥ jajñe revatyām dayitaḥ sutaḥ subhadrāyām rathī pārthāt abhimanyuḥ ajāyata akrūrāt kāśi kanyāyām satyaketuḥ ajāyata ye putrāḥ jajñire śūrāḥ namataḥ tān nibodhata bhojaḥ ca vijayaḥ ca eva śāntidevā sutau ubhau vṛkadevaḥ sunāmāyām gadaḥ ca asyāḥ sutau ubhau agāvaham mahātmānam vṛkadevī vyajāyata kanyā trigarta rājasya bhartā vai śiśirāyaṇaḥ gopālī tu apsarāḥ tasya gopa strī veṣa dhāriṇī mānuṣyām gargya bhāryāyām niyogāt śūlapāṇinaḥ sa kālayavanaḥ nāma jajñe rājā mahā balaḥ vṛṣa pūrva ardha kāyāḥ tam avahan vājinaḥ raṇe aputrasya sa rājñaḥ tu vavṛdhe antaḥpure śiśuḥ dūtam ca preṣayām āsa vṛṣṇi andhaka niveśane tatas vṛṣṇi andhakāḥ kṛṣṇam puraskṛtya mahāmatim vihāya mathurām ramyām mānayantaḥ pinākinam kuśasthalīm dvāravatīm niveśayitum īpsavaḥ iti kṛṣṇasya janma idam yaḥ śuciḥ niyata indriyaḥ parvasu śrāvayet vidvān nirṛṇaḥ sa sukhī bhavet uvāca kroṣṭoḥ eva abhavat putraḥ vṛjinīvant mahā yaśāḥ vārjinīvatam icchanti svāhim svāhākṛtām varam svāhi putraḥ abhavat rājā ruṣadguḥ vadatām varaḥ mahā kratubhiḥ īje yaḥ vividhaiḥ āpta dakṣiṇaiḥ āsīt caitrarathiḥ vīraḥ yajvā vipula dakṣiṇaḥ śaśabinduḥ param vṛttam rājarṣīṇām anuṣṭhitaḥ pṛthuśravāḥ pṛthuyaśāḥ rājā āsīt śāśabindu jaḥ śaṃsanti ca purāṇa jñāḥ pārthaśravasam antaram uṣataḥ yajñam akhilam svadharmam uṣatām varaḥ śineyuḥ abhavat putraḥ uṣataḥ śatru tāpanaḥ nihatya rukmakavacaḥ śatam kavacinām raṇe dhanvinām niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ avāpa śriyam uttamām jajñire pañca putrāḥ tu mahā vīryāḥ parājitāḥ rukmeṣuḥ pṛthurukmaḥ ca jyāmaghaḥ pālitaḥ hariḥ rukmeṣuḥ abhavat rājā pṛthurukmaḥ ca saṃśritaḥ tābhyām pravrājitaḥ rājyāt jyāmaghaḥ avasat āśrame praśāntaḥ sa vanasthaḥ tu brāhmaṇena avabodhitaḥ jagāma ratham āsthāya deśam anyam dhvajī rathī narmadā kūlam ekākī narmadām mṛttikāvatīm ṛkṣavantam girim jitvā śuktimatyām uvāsa saḥ bhāryā caitrā pariṇatā satī aputraḥ api ca rājā sa na anyām bhāryām avindata bhāryām uvāca saṃtrāsāt snuṣā iti sa nareśvaraḥ ugreṇa tapasā tasyāḥ kanyāyāḥ sā vyajāyata putryām vidarbham subhāgā caitrā pariṇatā satī rāja putryām tu vidvasau snuṣāyām kratha kaiśikau paścāt vidarbhaḥ ajanayat śūrau raṇa viśāradau kunteḥ dhṛṣṭaḥ sutaḥ jajñe raṇa dhṛṣṭaḥ pratāpavān dhṛṣṭasya jajñire śūrāḥ trayaḥ parama dhārmikāḥ āvantaḥ ca daśārhaḥ ca balī viṣṇu haraḥ ca yaḥ daśārhasya sutaḥ vyomā vidvān jīmūtaḥ ucyate jīmūta putraḥ vṛkatiḥ tasya bhīmarathaḥ sutaḥ tasya ca āsīt daśarathaḥ śakuniḥ tasya ca ātmajaḥ madhūnām vaṃśa kṛt rājā madhuḥ madhura vāc api mātā jajñe atha vaidarbhyām bhadravatyām kuru udvaha pārthivā ca abhavat bhāryā mātuḥ tasyām ajāyata sarva sattva guṇa upetaḥ sātvatām kīrti vardhanaḥ imām visṛṣṭim vijñāya jyāmaghasya mahātmanaḥ yujyate parayā prītyā prajāvān ca bhavati uta uvāca bhajinam bhajamānam ca divyam devāvṛdham nṛpam andhakam ca mahā bāhum vṛṣṇim ca yadu nandanam teṣām visargāḥ catvāraḥ vistareṇa iha tāṅ śṛṇu bhajamānasya sṛñjayyau bāhyakā ca upabāhyakā bhārye tayoḥ tasmāt jajñire bahavaḥ sutāḥ nimiḥ ca kramaṇaḥ ca eva viṣṇuḥ śūraḥ puraṃjayaḥ ete bāhyaka sṛñjayyām bhajamānāt vijajñire māyutājit sahasrājit śatājit ca atha dāsakaḥ upabāhyaka sṛñjayyām bhajamānāt vijajñire yajvā devāvṛdhaḥ rājā cacāra vipulam tapaḥ saṃyujya ātmānam evam sa parṇāśāyāḥ jalam spṛśan cintayā abhiparītā sā jagāma eka viniścayam na adhyagacchata tām nārīm yasyām evaṃvidhaḥ sutaḥ atha bhūtvā kumārī sā bibhratī paramam vapuḥ āsa nṛpatim tām iyeṣa ca sa prabhuḥ atha sā daśame māsi suṣuve saritām varā putram sarva guṇa upetam babhrum devāvṛdhāt nṛpāt anuvaṃśe purāṇa jñāḥ gāyanti iti pariśrutam guṇān devāvṛdhasya atha kīrtayantaḥ mahātmanaḥ yathā eva agre śrutam dūrāt apaśyāma tathā antikāt babhruḥ śreṣṭhaḥ manuṣyāṇām devaiḥ devāvṛdhaḥ samaḥ ṣaṣṭiḥ ca ṣaṭ ca puruṣāḥ sahasrāṇi ca sapta ca ete amṛta tvam saṃprāptāḥ babhroḥ daivāvṛdhāt iti yajvā dānapatiḥ dhīmān brahmaṇyaḥ su dṛḍha āyudhaḥ tasya anvavāyaḥ su mahān bhojāḥ ye mārtikāvatāḥ andhakāt kāśya duhitā caturaḥ alabhata ātmajān kukuram bhajamānam ca śamim kambalabarhiṣam kukurasya sutaḥ dhṛṣṇuḥ dhṛṣṇoḥ tu tanayaḥ tathā āhukaḥ ca āhukī ca eva khyātau khyātimatām varau imāḥ ca udāharanti atra gāthāḥ prati tam āhukam aśīti carmaṇā yuktaḥ na āhukaḥ prathamam vrajet na a putravān na a śata daḥ na a sahasra śata āyudhaḥ pūrvasyām diśi nāgānām bhojasya iti anumodanam rūpya kāñcana kakṣyāṇām sahasrāṇi daśa api ca tāvanti eva sahasrāṇi uttarasyām tathā diśi ā bhūmipālān bhojān svān atiṣṭhan kiṃkiṇīkinaḥ māhukīm ca api avantibhyaḥ svasāram daduḥ andhakāḥ māhukasya tu kāśyāyām dvau putrau saṃbabhūvatuḥ devakasya abhavan putrāḥ catvāraḥ tridaśa upamāḥ kumāryaḥ sapta ca api āsan vasudevāya tāḥ dadau devakī śāntidevā ca sudevā devarakṣitā navā ugrasenasya sutāḥ teṣām kaṃsaḥ tu pūrvajaḥ nyagrodhaḥ ca sunāmā ca kaṅku śaṅku subhūmayaḥ rāṣṭrapālaḥ atha sutanuḥ anādhṛṣṭiḥ ca puṣṭimant eṣām svasāraḥ pañca āsan kaṃsā kaṃsavatī tathā sutanuḥ rāṣṭrapālī ca kaṅkā ca eva vara aṅganā kukurāṇām imam vaṃśam dhārayan amita ojasām ātmanaḥ vipulam vaṃśam prajāvān āpnute naraḥ uvāca rājādhidevaḥ śūraḥ tu vidūratha sutaḥ abhavat rājādhidevasya sutāḥ jajñire vīryavattarāḥ balinaḥ śoṇāśvaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ śamī ca daṇḍaśarmā ca dattaśatruḥ ca śatrujit śravaṇā ca śraviṣṭhā ca svasārau saṃbabhūvatuḥ śamī putraḥ pratikṣatraḥ pratikṣatrasya ca ātmajaḥ svayaṃbhojaḥ svayambhojāt dhṛdikaḥ saṃbabhūva ha tasya putrāḥ babhūvuḥ hi sarve bhīma parākramāḥ kṛtavarmā agrajaḥ teṣām śatadhanvā tu madhyamaḥ devāntaḥ ca narāntaḥ ca bhiṣaj vaitaraṇaḥ ca yaḥ sudāntaḥ ca adhidāntaḥ ca kīnāśaḥ dāma dambhakau asamaujāḥ tathā vīraḥ nāsamaujāḥ ca tau ubhau sudaṃṣṭram ca sucārum ca kṛṣṇam iti andhakāḥ smṛtāḥ gāndhārī ca eva mādrī ca kroṣṭoḥ bhārye babhūvatuḥ gāndhārī janayām āsa sumitram mitra nandanam mādrī yudhājitam putram tatas vai devamīḍhuṣam anamitram amitrāṇām jetāram ca mahā balam prasenaḥ dvāravatyām tu niviśatyām mahā maṇim sa maṇiḥ syandate rukmam vṛṣṇi andhaka niveśane kadācid mṛgayām yātaḥ prasenaḥ tena bhūṣitaḥ syamantaka kṛte siṃhāt vadham prāpa vanecarāt atha siṃham pradhāvantam ṛkṣa rājaḥ mahā balaḥ nihatya maṇi ratnam tam ādāya bilam āviśat tatas vṛṣṇi andhakāḥ kṛṣṇam prasena vadha kāraṇāt prārthanām tām maṇeḥ buddhvā sarve eva śaśaṅkire sa śaṅkyamānaḥ dharma ātmā nakārī tasya karmaṇaḥ maṇim iti pratijñāya vanam yayau prasenasya padam gṛhya puruṣaiḥ āpta kāribhiḥ anveṣayan pariśrāntaḥ sa dadarśa mahā manāḥ sa aśvam hatam prasenam tu na avindat ca eva tam maṇim atha siṃhaḥ prasenasya śarīrasya avidūrataḥ ṛkṣeṇa nihataḥ dṛṣṭaḥ pādaiḥ ṛkṣasya sūcitaḥ pādaiḥ taiḥ anviyāya atha guhām ṛkṣasya mādhavaḥ mahati ṛkṣa bile vāṇīm śuśrāva pramadā īritām dhātryā kumāram ādāya sutam jāmbavataḥ nṛpa mā rodīḥ iti atha īritām uvāca siṃhaḥ prasenam avadhīt siṃhaḥ jāmbavatā hataḥ vyaktīkṛtaḥ ca śabdaḥ saḥ tūrṇam ca api yayau bilam śārṅgadhanvā bila stham tu jāmbavantam dadarśa ha praviṣṭe tu bilam kṛṣṇe vasudeva puraḥsarāḥ punar dvāravatīm etya hatam kṛṣṇam nyavedayan lebhe jāmbavatīm kanyām ṛkṣa rājasya saṃmatām anunīya ṛkṣa rājānam niryayau ca tadā bilāt evam sa maṇim āhṛtya viśodhya ātmānam acyutaḥ evam mithyā abhiśastena kṛṣṇena amitra ghātinā ātmā viśodhitaḥ pāpāt vinirjitya syamantakam satrājitaḥ daśa tu āsan bhāryāḥ tāsām śatam sutāḥ khyātimantaḥ trayaḥ teṣām bhaṅgakāraḥ tu pūrvajaḥ ca eva tathā eva ca kumāryaḥ ca api tisraḥ vai dikṣu khyātāḥ narādhipa satyabhāmā uttamā strīṇām vratinī ca dṛḍha vratā tathā padmāvatī ca eva bhāryāḥ kṛṣṇasya tāḥ dadau sabhākṣaḥ bhaṅgakārāt tu nāreyaḥ ca nara uttamau jajñāte guṇa saṃpannau viśrutau guṇa saṃpadā madhoḥ putrasya jajñe atha pṛśniḥ putraḥ yudhājitaḥ jajñāte tanayau pṛśneḥ śvaphalkaḥ citrakaḥ tathā śvaphalkaḥ kāśi rājasya sutām bhāryām avindata gāndīm tasyāḥ tu gāndī tvam sadā gāḥ pradadau hi sā tasyām jajñe tadā vīraḥ śrutavant iti bhārata akrūraḥ atha mahābhāgaḥ yajvā vipula dakṣiṇaḥ upāsaṅgaḥ tathā madguḥ mṛduraḥ ca arimardanaḥ girikṣipaḥ tathā upekṣaḥ śatru hā ca arimejayaḥ carmabhṛt ca arivarmā ca gṛdhram ojāḥ naraḥ tathā māvāha prativāhau ca sundarā ca vara aṅganā viśrutā sāmba mahiṣī kanyā ca asya vasuṃdharā akrūreṇa augrasenyām tu su gātrāyām kuru nandana aśvasenaḥ aśvabāhuḥ ca supārśvaka gaveṣaṇau subāhuḥ bahubāhuḥ ca śraviṣṭḥ āśravaṇe striyau imām mithyā abhiśastim yaḥ kṛṣṇasya samudāhṛtām veda mithyā abhiśāpāḥ tam na spṛśanti kadācana uvāca sadā hi prārthayām āsa satyabhāmām aninditām satrājitam tatas hatvā śatadhanvā mahā balaḥ rātrau tam maṇim ādāya tatas akrūrāya dattavan samayam samayam kārayām cakre na āvedyaḥ aham tvayā acyute vayam abhyupapatsyāmaḥ kṛṣṇena tvām pradharṣitam mama adya dvārakā sarvā vaśe tiṣṭhati asaṃśayam hate pitare duḥkha ārtā satyabhāmā yaśasvinī bhartuḥ nivedya duḥkha ārtā pārśva sthā aśrūṇi avartayat pāṇḍavānām tu dagdhānām hariḥ kṛtvā udakam tadā kulya arthe ca sa bhrātṝṇām nyayojayata sātyakim tatas tvaritam āgamya dvārakām madhusūdanaḥ pūrvajam halinam śrīmān idam vacanam abravīt tadā āroha ratham śīghram bhojam hatvā mahā balam tatas pravavṛte yuddham tumulam bhoja kṛṣṇayoḥ śaktaḥ api śāṭhyāt dhārdikyam na akrūraḥ abhyupapadyata yojanānām śatam sāgram hayayā pratyapadyata vikhyātā hṛdayā nāma śata yojana gāminī bhojasya vaḍavā rājan yayā kṛṣṇam ayodhayat kṣīṇām javena hṛdayām adhvanaḥ śata yojane dṛṣṭvā rathasya svām vṛddhim śatadhanvānam ārdayat tatas tasyāḥ hayāyāḥ tu śramāt khedāt ca bhārata utpetuḥ atha prāṇāḥ kṛṣṇaḥ rāmam atha abravīt tiṣṭhasva iha mahā bāho dṛṣṭa doṣā hayā mayā padbhyām gatvā hariṣyāmi maṇi ratnam syamantakam nivṛttam ca abravīt kṛṣṇam ratnam dehi iti lāṅgalī na asti iti kṛṣṇaḥ ca uvāca tatas rāmaḥ ruṣā anvitaḥ bhrātṛ tvāt marṣayāmi eṣa svasti te astu vrajāmi aham mama dvārakayā na tvayā na ca vṛṣṇibhiḥ nānā rūpān kratūn sarvān ājahāra nirargalān dīkṣā mayam sa kavacam rakṣā artham praviveśa ha syamantaka kṛte prājñaḥ gāndī putraḥ mahā yaśāḥ arthān ratnāni ca agryāṇi dravyāṇi vividhāni ca ṣaṣṭim varṣāṇi dharma ātmā yajñeṣu viniyojayat akrūra yajñāḥ iti te khyātāḥ tasya mahātmanaḥ bahu anna dakṣiṇāḥ sarve sarva kāma pradāyinaḥ atha duryodhanaḥ rājā gatvā sa mithilām prabhuḥ gadā śikṣām tatas divyām balabhadrāt avāptavan prasādya tu tatas rāmaḥ vṛṣṇi andhaka mahā rathaiḥ mahātmanā hatvā satrājitam yuddhe sahabandhum mahā balī jñāti bheda bhayāt kṛṣṇaḥ tam upekṣitavan atha apayāte tadā akrūre na avarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ anāvṛṣṭyā tadā rāṣṭram abhavat bahudhā kṛśam tatas prasādayām āsuḥ akrūram kukura andhakāḥ kanyām ca vāsudevāya svasāram śīla saṃmatām atha vijñāya yogena kṛṣṇaḥ babhru gatam maṇim sabhā madhya gatam prāha tam akrūram janārdanaḥ tat prayacchasva māna arha mayi mā anāryakam kṛthāḥ bhūt tadā mama sa saṃrūḍhaḥ asakṛt prāptaḥ tatas kāla atyayaḥ mahān tatas kṛṣṇasya vacanāt sarva sātvata saṃsadi pradadau tam maṇim babhruḥ akleśena mahāmatiḥ dadau hṛṣṭa manāḥ kṛṣṇaḥ tam maṇim babhrave punar sa kṛṣṇa hastāt saṃprāpya maṇi ratnam syamantakam ābadhya gāndinī putraḥ virarāja aṃśumant iva vistareṇa eva sarvāṇi karmāṇi ripu ghātinaḥ śrotum icchāmi aśeṣeṇa hareḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ karmaṇām ānupūrvyā ca prādurbhāvāḥ ca ye vibhoḥ yā ca asya prakṛtiḥ brahman tām ca vyākhyātum arhasi katham ca bhagavant viṣṇuḥ sureśaḥ ari niṣūdanaḥ amaraiḥ āvṛtam puṇyam puṇya kṛdbhiḥ alaṃkṛtam kimartham divvyam ātmānam mānuṣye saṃnyayojayat yaḥ cakram vartayati ekaḥ mānuṣāṇām anāmayam mānuṣye sa katham buddhim cakre cakra bhṛtām varaḥ mahābhūtāni bhūtātmā yaḥ dadhāra cakāra ca śrīgarbhaḥ sa katham garbhe striyā bhū carayā dhṛtaḥ yaḥ antakāle jagant pītvā kṛtvā toya mayam vapuḥ lokam ekārṇavam cakre dṛśya a dṛśyeṇa vartmanā yaḥ purāṇe purāṇa ātmā vārāham vapuḥ āsthitaḥ ujjahāra dadau jitvā vasumatīm surāṇām sura sattamaḥ yena saiṃham vapuḥ kṛtvā dvidhā kṛtvā ca tat punar pūrva daityaḥ mahā vīryaḥ hiraṇyakaśipuḥ hataḥ yaḥ purā hi analaḥ bhūtvā aurvaḥ saṃvartakaḥ vibhuḥ pātāla sthaḥ arṇava gatam papau toya mayam haviḥ sahasra caraṇam brahman sahasra aṃśum sahasraśas nābhi araṇau samutpannam yasya paitāmaham gṛham yena te nihatāḥ daityāḥ saṃgrāme tārakā maye sarva deva mayam kṛtvā sarva āyudha dharam vapuḥ uttara ante samudrasya kṣīrodasya amṛta udadheḥ yaḥ śete śāśvatam yogam āsthāya timiram mahat surāraṇiḥ garbham adhatta divyam tapaḥ prakarṣāt aditiḥ purāṇam śakram ca yaḥ daitya gaṇa avaruddham garbha avasāne na kṛśam cakāra padāni yaḥ loka padāni kṛtvā cakāra daityān salilāśaya sthān kṛtvā ca devān tridivasya devān cakre sura īśam puruhūtam eva patyena vidhinā anvāhāryeṇa karmaṇā agnim āhavanīyam ca vedīm ca eva kuśān sruvam prokṣaṇīyam dhruvām ca eva āvabhṛthyam tathā eva ca havya ādān ca surān cakre kavya ādān ca pitṝn api bhāga arthe yajña vidhinā yoga jñaḥ yajña karmaṇi yūpān samidh srucam somam pavitram paridhīn api yajñiyāni ca dravyāṇi yajñān ca cayana analān sadasyāni ajamānān ca medha ādīn ca kratu uttamān vibabhāja purā yaḥ ca pārameṣṭhyena karmaṇā yuga anurūpam yaḥ kṛtvā lokān anu parikraman kṣaṇāḥ nimeṣāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ ca kalāḥ traikālyam eva ca muhūrtāḥ tithayaḥ māsāḥ dina saṃvatsarāḥ tathā ṛtavaḥ kāla yogāḥ ca pramāṇam vividham nṛṣu āyuḥ kṣetrāṇi upacayaḥ lakṣaṇam rūpa sauṣṭhavam trayaḥ varṇāḥ trayaḥ lokāḥ traividyam pāvakāḥ trayaḥ traikālyam trīṇi karmāṇi trayaḥ apāyāḥ trayaḥ guṇāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ lokāḥ trayaḥ anantāḥ yena ānantyena vartmanā sarva bhūta guṇa sraṣṭā sarva bhūta guṇa ātmakaḥ nṛṇām indriya pūrveṇa yogena ramate ca yaḥ yaḥ netā tatra iha ca vidhi īśvaraḥ yaḥ gatiḥ dharma yuktānām agatiḥ pāpa karmaṇām cāturvarṇyasya prabhavaḥ cāturvarṇyasya rakṣitā cāturvidyasya yaḥ vettā cāturāśramya saṃśrayaḥ candra sūrya dvayam jyotiḥ yogi īśaḥ kṣaṇadā tanuḥ yaḥ param śrūyate jyotiḥ yaḥ param śrūyate tapaḥ yaḥ param prāha paratas param yaḥ parama ātmavān yuga anteṣu antakaḥ yaḥ ca yaḥ ca loka antaka antakaḥ soma bhūtaḥ ca bhūtānām agni bhūtaḥ agni varcasām manuṣyāṇām manaḥ bhūtaḥ tapaḥ bhūtaḥ tapasvinām sarga kāraḥ ca sargāṇām loka hetuḥ anuttamaḥ ākāśa prabhavaḥ vāyuḥ vāyu prāṇaḥ hutāśanaḥ devāḥ hutāśana prāṇāḥ prāṇaḥ agneḥ madhusūdanaḥ rasāt vai śoṇitam bhavati śoṇitāt māṃsam ucyate asthinaḥ majjā samabhavat majjāyāḥ śukra saṃbhavaḥ śukrāt na ṛbhaḥ samabhavat rasa mūlena karmaṇā tatra apām prathamaḥ bhāgaḥ sa saumyaḥ rāśiḥ ucyate śukram soma ātmakam vidyāt ārtavam pāvaka ātmakam bhāvau rasa anugau etau vīryam ca śaśi pāvakau kaphasya hṛdayam sthānam nābhyām pittam pratiṣṭhitam nābhi kaṇṭha antara sthaḥ tu tatra devaḥ hutāśanaḥ praveśanam cakre saṃgataḥ paramātmanā prāṇa apānau samānaḥ ca udānaḥ vyānaḥ eva ca apānaḥ paścimam kāyam udāna ūrdhvam śarīriṇaḥ pṛthivī vāyuḥ ākāśam apaḥ jyotiḥ ca pañcamam tasya indriyāṇi śiṣṭāni svam svam yogam pracakrire pārthivam deham āhuḥ tu prāṇa ātmānam ca mārutam chidrāṇi ākāśa yonīni jala srāvaḥ pravartate jyotiḥ cakṣuṣi tejaḥ ca teṣām yantṛ manaḥ smṛtam grāmyāḥ ca viṣayāḥ ca eva yasya vīryāt pravartitāḥ iti etān puruṣaḥ sarvān sṛjan lokān sanātanān katham gatiḥ gatimatām āpannaḥ mānuṣīm tanum śrutaḥ me svasya vaṃśasya pūrvajānām ca saṃbhavaḥ śrotum icchāmi viṣṇoḥ tu vṛṣṇīnām ca yathākramam āścaryam paramam viṣṇuḥ devaiḥ daityaiḥ ca kathyate viṣṇoḥ utpattim āścaryam mama ācakṣva mahā mune etat āścaryam ākhyānam kathayasva sukha āvaham karmaṇā āścarya bhūtasya viṣṇoḥ tattvam iha ucyatām uvāca praśna bhāraḥ mahān tāta tvayā uktaḥ śārṅgadhanvani yathāśakti tu vakṣyāmi śrūyatām vaiṣṇavam yaśaḥ viṣṇoḥ prabhāva śravaṇe diṣṭyā te matiḥ utthitā hanta viṣṇoḥ samastāḥ tvam śṛṇu divyāḥ pravṛttayaḥ sahasra āsyam sahasra akṣam sahasra caraṇam ca yam pātrāṇi ca pavitrāṇi vedim dīkṣām carum sruvam upabhṛt prokṣaṇīm dakṣiṇāyanam yūpam samidh sruvam darvīm camasa ulūkhalāni ca prāgvaṃśam yajña bhūmim ca hotāram cayanam ca yat hrasvāni atipramāṇāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca prāyaścittāni ca arghyam ca sthaṇḍilāni kuśān tathā mantram yajña vaham vahnim bhāgam bhāga vaham ca yat āhuḥ veda vidaḥ viprāḥ yam yajñam śāśvatam vibhum tasya viṣṇoḥ sureśasya śrīvatsa aṅkasya dhīmataḥ prādurbhāva sahasrāṇi samatītāni anekaśas bhūyas ca eva bhaviṣyanti iti evam āha pitāmahaḥ yat pṛcchasi mahā rāja divyām puṇyām kathām śubhām tat te aham saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇu sarvam aśeṣatas vāsudevasya māhātmyam caritam ca mahā dyuteḥ hita artham sura martyānām lokānām prabhavāya ca bahuśas sarva bhūta ātmā prādurbhavati kāryataḥ prādurbhāvān ca vakṣyāmi puṇyān deva guṇaiḥ yutān devāḥ saptarṣayaḥ ca eva tryambakaḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ sanatkumāraḥ ca mahā anubhāvaḥ manuḥ mahātmā bhagavān prajā karaḥ purāṇa devaḥ atha purāṇi cakre pradīpta vaiśvānara tulya tejāḥ naṣṭe deva asura nare pranaṣṭa uraga rākṣase puṣkare yatra saṃbhūtāḥ devāḥ sa ṛṣi gaṇāḥ purā eṣa pauṣkarakaḥ nāma prādurbhāvaḥ prakīrtitaḥ vārāhaḥ tu śruti sukhaḥ prādurbhāvaḥ mahātmanaḥ yatra viṣṇuḥ suraśreṣṭhaḥ vārāham rūpam āsthitaḥ yūpa daṃṣṭraḥ kratu dantaḥ citī mukhaḥ agni jihvaḥ darbha lomā brahma śīrṣaḥ mahā tapāḥ ahorātra īkṣaṇaḥ divyaḥ vedāṅga śruti bhūṣaṇaḥ ājya nāsaḥ sruvaḥ tuṇḍaḥ sāma ghoṣa svanaḥ mahān prāyaścitta nakhaḥ dhīraḥ paśu jānuḥ mahāvṛṣaḥ udgātṛ āntraḥ homa liṅgaḥ phala bīja mahauṣadhī vāyu antarātmā mantra sphic vikṛtaḥ soma śoṇitaḥ prāc vaṃśa kāyaḥ dyutimān nānā dīkṣābhiḥ ācitaḥ dakṣiṇā hṛdayaḥ yogī mahā sattra mayaḥ mahān pravargya āvarta bhūṣaṇaḥ chāyā patnī sahāyaḥ vai maṇi śṛṅge iva ucchritaḥ mahīm sāgara paryantām sa śaila vana kānanām ekārṇava jale bhraṣṭām ekārṇava gatiḥ prabhuḥ daṃṣṭrayā yaḥ samuddhṛtya lokānām hita kāmyayā sahasra śīrṣaḥ deva ādiḥ cakāra jagatīm punar evam yajñavarāhena bhūtvā bhūta hita arthinā uddhṛtā pṛthivī devī sāgara ambudharā purā mārāhaḥ eṣa kathitaḥ nārasiṃham atas śṛṇu yatra bhūtvā mṛgendreṇa hiraṇyakaśipuḥ hataḥ daityānām ādipuruṣaḥ cakāra tapaḥ uttamam daśa varśa sahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca jala upavāsaḥ tasya āsīt sthāna mauna dṛḍha vrataḥ tatas śama damābhyām ca brahmacaryeṇa ca anagha rudraiḥ viśva sahāyaiḥ ca yakṣa rākṣasa kiṃnaraiḥ diśābhiḥ vidiśābhiḥ ca nadībhiḥ sāgaraiḥ tathā nakṣatraiḥ ca muhūrtaiḥ ca khecaraiḥ ca mahāgrahaiḥ carācara guruḥ śrīmān vṛtaḥ sarvaiḥ suraiḥ tathā brahmā brahma vidām śreṣṭhaḥ daityam vacanam abravīt varaya varaya bhadram te yathā iṣṭam kāmam āpnuhi uvāca na deva asura gandharvāḥ na yakṣa uraga rākṣsāḥ na mānuṣāḥ piśācāḥ vā hanyuḥ mām deva sattamaiḥ ṛṣayaḥ vā na mām śāpaiḥ kruddhāḥ lokapitāmahaiḥ śapeyuḥ tapasā yuktāḥ varam etam vṛṇomi aham na śastreṇa na ca astreṇa giriṇā pādapena vā na śuṣkeṇa na ca ārdreṇa syāt na ca anyena me vadhaḥ bhaveyam aham eva arkaḥ somaḥ vāyuḥ hutāśanaḥ salilam ca antarikṣam ca nakṣatrāṇi diśaḥ daśa aham krodhaḥ ca kāmaḥ ca varuṇaḥ vāsavaḥ yamaḥ dhanadaḥ ca dhanādhyakṣaḥ yakṣaḥ kiṃpuruṣa adhipaḥ ete divyāḥ varāḥ tāta mayā dattāḥ tava adbhutāḥ sarvān kāmān imān tāta prāpsyasi tvam na saṃśayaḥ evam uktvā tu bhagavān jagāma ākāśam eva ha tatas devāḥ ca nāgāḥ ca gandharvāḥ munayaḥ tathā eva ūcuḥ bhagavān sarva bhūtānām svayambhuḥ ādi kṛt vibhuḥ sraṣṭā ca havya kavyānām avyaktaḥ prakṛtiḥ dhruvaḥ tatas loka hitam vākyam śrutvā devaḥ prajāpatiḥ provāca bhagavān vākyam sarvān deva gaṇān tadā avaśyam tridaśāḥ tena prāptavyam tapasaḥ phalam etat śrutvā surāḥ sarve vākyam paṅkaja janmanaḥ svāni sthānāni divyāni jagmuḥ te vai mudā yutāḥ labdha mātre vare ca api sarvāḥ saḥ abādhata prajāḥ mahābhāgān munīn vai saṃśita vratān satya dharma ratān dāntān purā dharṣitavan tu saḥ devān tribhuvana sthān ca parājitya mahā asuraḥ trailokyam vaśam ānīya svarge vasati dānavaḥ yajñiyān akarot daityān a yajñīyāḥ ca devatāḥ ādityāḥ ca tatas sādhyāḥ viśvāḥ atha vasavaḥ tathā śaraṇyam śaraṇam viṣṇum upatasthuḥ mahā balam nārāyaṇam vibhuḥ devāḥ śaraṇyam śaraṇyam gatāḥ tvam hi naḥ paramaḥ dhātā brahma ādīnām sura uttamaiḥ utphulla ambuja pattra akṣa śatru pakṣa bhaya āvaha kṣayāya diti vaṃśasya śaraṇam tvam bhavasva naḥ uvāca eṣaḥ aham sa gaṇam daityam vara dānena darpitam evam uktvā saḥ bhagavant visṛjya tridaśa īśvarān hiraṇyakaśipoḥ rājan ājagāma hariḥ sabhām narasya kṛtvā ardha tanum siṃhasya ardha tanum tathā nārasiṃhena vapuṣā pāṇim saṃspṛśya pāṇinā jīmūta ghana saṃkāśaḥ jīmūta ghana nisvanaḥ jīmūta ghana dīpta ojāḥ jīmūtaḥ iva vegavān daityam saḥ atibalam dṛptam dṛpta śārdūla vikramam dṛptaiḥ daitya gaṇaiḥ guptam hatavan eka pāṇinā nṛsiṃhaḥ eṣa kathitaḥ bhūyas ayam vāmanaḥ aparaḥ yatra vāmanam āśritya rūpam daitya vināśanam baleḥ balavataḥ yajñe balinā viṣṇunā purā vikramaiḥ tribhiḥ akṣobhyāḥ kṣobhitāḥ te mahā asurāḥ vipracittiḥ śibiḥ śaṅkuḥ ayaḥśaṅkuḥ tathā eva ca ayaḥśirāḥ aśvaśirāḥ hayagrīvaḥ ca vīryavān puṣkaraḥ puṣkalaḥ ca eva sa aśvaḥ aśvapatiḥ eva ca prahrādaḥ aśvaśirāḥ kumbhaḥ saṃhrādaḥ gaganapriyaḥ śarabhaḥ śalabhaḥ ca eva kupanaḥ kopanaḥ krathaḥ mahā kīrtiḥ mahā jihvaḥ śaṅku karṇaḥ mahā svanaḥ vāyuḥ gaviṣṭhaḥ namuciḥ śambaraḥ vikṣaraḥ mahān kālakaḥ kālakeyaḥ ca vṛtraḥ krodhaḥ virocanaḥ gariṣṭhaḥ ca variṣṭhaḥ ca pralamba narakau ubhau yad indra tāpana vātāpī ketumant bala darpitaḥ asilomā pulomā ca bāṣkalaḥ pramadaḥ madaḥ khasṛmaḥ kālavadanaḥ karālaḥ keśiḥ eva ca eka akṣaḥ candra hā rāhuḥ saṃhrādaḥ sṛmaraḥ svanaḥ śataghnī cakra hastāḥ ca tathā parigha pāṇayaḥ aśma yantra āyudha upetāḥ bhindipāla āyudhāḥ tathā śūla ulūkhala hastāḥ ca paraśvadha dharāḥ tathā pāśa mudgara hastāḥ vai tathā laguḍa pāṇayaḥ mahā śilā praharaṇāḥ śūla hastāḥ ca dānavāḥ nānā praharaṇāḥ ghorāḥ nānā veṣāḥ mahā javāḥ kūrma kukkuṭa vaktrāḥ ca śaśa ulūka mukhāḥ tathā khara uṣṭra vadanāḥ ca eva varāha vadanāḥ tathā bhīmāḥ makara vaktrāḥ ca kroṣṭu vaktrāḥ ca dānavāḥ ca ghorāḥ vṛka mukhāḥ tathā mārjāra śaśa vaktrāḥ ca mahā vaktrāḥ tathā apare godhā śalyaka vaktrāḥ ca krauñca vaktrāḥ tathā apare garuḍa ānanāḥ khaḍga mukhāḥ mayūra vadanāḥ tathā gaja indra carma vasanāḥ tathā kṛṣṇa ajina ambarāḥ cīra saṃvṛta gātrāḥ ca tathā valkala vāsasaḥ uṣṇīṣiṇaḥ mukuṭinaḥ tathā kuṇḍalinaḥ asurāḥ kirīṭinaḥ lamba śikhāḥ kambu grīvāḥ su varcasaḥ nānā veṣa dharāḥ daityāḥ nānā mālya anulepanāḥ svāni āyudhāni saṃgṛhya pradīptāni iva tejasā kramamāṇam hṛṣīkeśam upāvartanta sarvaśas rūpam kṛtvā jahāra āśu saḥ medinīm nabhaḥ prakramamāṇasya nābhau kila samāsthitau viṣṇoḥ amita vīryasya vadanti evam dvijātayaḥ hṛtvā sa medinīm kṛtsnām hatvā ca asura puṃgavān dadau śakrāya vasudhām viṣṇuḥ balavatām varaḥ eṣa te vāmanaḥ nāma prādurbhāvaḥ mahātmanaḥ bhūyas bhūtātmanaḥ viṣṇoḥ prādurbhāvaḥ mahātmanaḥ dattātreyaḥ iti khyātaḥ kṣamayā parayā yutaḥ tena naṣṭeṣu deveṣu prakriyāsu makheṣu ca cāturvarṇye ca saṃkīrṇe dharme śithila tām gate prajāsu śīryamāṇāsu dharme ca ākula tām gate sa yajñāḥ sa kriyāḥ vedāḥ pratyānītāḥ hi tena vai cāturvarṇyam asaṃkīrṇam kṛtam tena mahātmanā śatāni daśa bāhūnām bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ pālayiṣyasi kṛtsnām ca vasudhām vasudhā īśvara durnirīkṣyaḥ ari vṛndānām yuddha sthaḥ ca bhaviṣyasi eṣa te vaiṣṇavaḥ śrīmān prādurbhāvaḥ adbhutaḥ śubhaḥ bhūyas ca jāmadagnyaḥ ayam prādurbhāvaḥ mahātmanaḥ rāmaḥ arjunam anīka stham jaghāna nṛpatim prabhuḥ ratha stham pārthivam rāmaḥ pātayitvā arjunam bhuvi dharṣayitvā yathākāmam krośamānam ca megha vat kīrṇā kṣatriya koṭībhiḥ meru mandara bhūṣaṇā tris sapta kṛtvas pṛthivī tena niḥkṣatriyā kṛtā kṛtvā niḥkṣatriyām ca eva bhārgavaḥ su mahā tapāḥ sarva pāpa vināśāya vājimedhena ca iṣṭavan tasmin yajñe mahā dāne dakṣiṇām bhṛgu nandanaḥ mārīcāya dadau prītaḥ kaśyapāya vasuṃdharām vāruṇān turagān śubhrān ratham ca rathinām varaḥ hiraṇyam akṣayam dhenūḥ gaja indrān ca mahāmatiḥ dadau tasmin mahā yajñe vājimedhe mahā yaśāḥ adya api ca hita arthāya lokānām bhṛgu nandanaḥ caramāṇaḥ tapaḥ dīptam jāmadagnyaḥ punar punar eṣa viṣṇoḥ sureśasya śāśvatasya avyayasya ca jāmadagnyaḥ iti khyātaḥ prādurbhāvaḥ mahātmanaḥ caturviṃśe yuge ca api viśvāmitra puraḥsaraḥ jajñe daśarathasya atha putraḥ padma āyata īkṣaṇaḥ kṛtvā ātmānam mahā bāhuḥ caturdhā prabhuḥ īśvaraḥ prasādana artham lokasya rakṣasām nigrahāya ca dharmasya ca vivṛddhi artham jajñe tatra mahā yaśāḥ tasmai dattāni ca astrāṇi viśvāmitreṇa dhīmatā vadha artham deva śatrūṇām durdharāṇi suraiḥ api yajña vighna karau yena munīnām bhāvitātmanām mārīcaḥ ca subāhuḥ ca balena balinām varau bhagnam māheśvaram cāpam krīḍatā līlayā purā lakṣmaṇa anucaraḥ rāmaḥ sarva bhūta hite rataḥ rūpiṇī yasya pārśva sthā sītā iti prathitā janaiḥ caturdaśa vane taptvā tapaḥ varṣāṇi rāghavaḥ janasthāne vasan kāryam tridaśānām cakāra saḥ sītāyāḥ padam anvicchan nijaghāna mahāmanāḥ sura indra vajra aśani tulya sāraiḥ śaraiḥ śarīreṣu viyojitau balāt bālī vinihataḥ saṃkhye sugrīvaḥ ca abhiṣecitaḥ deva asura gaṇānām hi yakṣa rākṣasa pakṣiṇām yatra avadhyam rākṣasa indram rāvaṇam yudhi durjayam rākṣasa koṭībhiḥ nīlāñjana caya upamam trailokya rāvaṇam krūram rākṣasam rākṣaseśvaram durjaram durdharam dṛptam śārdūla sama vikramam jaghāna sacivaiḥ sārdham sa sainyam rāvaṇam yudhi mahā abhra ghana saṃkāśam mahā kāyam mahā balam tam āgaskāriṇam krūram paulastyam puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ rāvaṇam nijaghāna āśu rāmaḥ bhūtapatiḥ purā madhoḥ ca tanayaḥ dṛptaḥ lavaṇaḥ nāma dānavaḥ samare yuddha śauṇḍena tathā anye ca api rākṣasāḥ etāni kṛtvā karmāṇi rāmaḥ dharma bhṛtām varaḥ daśa aśvamedhān jārūthyān ājahāra nirargalān na aśrūyanta aśubhāḥ vācaḥ na ākulam mārutaḥ vavau na vitta haraṇam ca āsīt rāme rājyam praśāsati sarvam āsīt jagat dāntam rāme rājyam praśāsati na prāṇinām bhayam ca āsīt jala anala vighāta jam na ca sma vṛddhāḥ bālānām pretakāryāṇi kurvate brahma paryat carat kṣatram viśaḥ kṣatram anuvratāḥ śūdrāḥ ca eva hi varṇān trīn śuśrūṣanti anahaṃkṛtāḥ nāryaḥ na atyacaran bhartṝn bhāryām na atyacarat patiḥ rāmaḥ ekaḥ abhavat bhartā rāmaḥ pālayitā abhavat āsan varṣa sahasrāṇi tathā putra sahasriṇaḥ arogāḥ prāṇinaḥ ca āsan rāme rājyam praśāsati devatānām ṛṣīṇām ca manuṣyāṇām ca sarvaśas pṛthivyām sahavāsaḥ abhūt rāme rājyam praśāsati gāthāḥ api atra gāyanti ye purāṇa vidaḥ janāḥ rāme nibaddhāḥ tattva arthāḥ māhātmyam tasya dhīmataḥ śyāmaḥ yuvā lohita akṣaḥ dīpta āsyaḥ mita bhāṣitā sumukhaḥ siṃha skandhaḥ mahā bhujaḥ daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi daśa varṣa śatāni ca ayodhyā adhipatiḥ bhūtvā rāmaḥ rājyam akārayat ṛk sāma yajuṣām ghoṣaḥ jyā ghoṣaḥ ca mahātmanaḥ avyucchinnaḥ abhavat rāṣṭre dīyatām bhujyatām iti sattvavān guṇa saṃpannaḥ dīpyamānaḥ sva tejasā ati sūryam ca candram ca rāmaḥ dāśarathiḥ babhau samāpta vara dākṣiṇaiḥ hitvā ayodhyām divam yātaḥ rāghavaḥ asau mahā balaḥ evam eṣa mahā bāhuḥ ikṣvāku kula nandanaḥ rāvaṇam sa gaṇam hatvā divam ācakrame prabhuḥ aparaḥ keśavasya ayam prādurbhāvaḥ mahātmanaḥ ariṣṭam vṛṣabham keśim pūtanām daitya dārikām nāgam kuvalayāpīḍam cāṇūram muṣṭikam tathā daityān mānuṣa deha sthān sūdayām āsa vīryavān chinnam bāhu sahasram ca bāṇasya adbhuta karmaṇaḥ narakaḥ ca hataḥ saṃkhye yavanaḥ ca mahā balaḥ hṛtāni ca mahīpānām sarva ratnāni tejasā durācārāḥ ca nihatāḥ pārthivāḥ ye mahī tale ete loka hita arthāya prādurbhāvāḥ mahātmanaḥ kalkī viṣṇuyaśāḥ nāma bhūyas ca utpatsyate prabhuḥ prādurbhāvāḥ purāṇeṣu gīyante brahma vādibhiḥ etat uddeśa mātreṇa prādurbhāva anukīrtanam viṣṇoḥ amita vīryasya yaḥ śṛṇoti kṛtāñjaliḥ etāḥ tu yogeśvara yoga māyāḥ śrutvā naraḥ mucyati sarva pāpaiḥ ṛddhim samṛddhim vipulān ca bhogān prāpnoti śīghram bhagavat prasādāt uvāca mama viṣṇoḥ hari tvam ca kṛte yuge vaikuṇṭha tvam ca deveṣu kṛṣṇa tvam mānuṣeṣu ca īśvarasya hi tasya imām karmaṇām gahanām gatim saṃprati atītām bhāvyām ca śṛṇu rājan yathātatham eṣa nārāyaṇaḥ bhūtvā hariḥ āsīt sanātanaḥ brahmā śakraḥ ca somaḥ ca dharmaḥ śukraḥ bṛhaspatiḥ pradhāna ātmā purā hi eṣa brahmāṇam asṛjat prabhuḥ saḥ asṛjat pūrvapuruṣaḥ purā kalpe prajāpatīn te tanvānāḥ tanūḥ tatra brahma vaṃśān anuttamān etat āścarya bhūtasya viṣṇoḥ karma anukīrtanam kīrtitam kīrtanīyasya kīrtyamānam nibodha mama āsīt trailokya vikhyātaḥ saṃgrāmaḥ tārakā mayaḥ tatra sma dānavāḥ ghorāḥ sarve saṃgrāma darpitāḥ te vadhyamānāḥ vimukhāḥ kṣīṇa praharaṇāḥ raṇe trātāram manasā jagmuḥ devam nārāyaṇam prabhum etasmin antare meghāḥ nirvāṇa aṅgāra varcasaḥ cañcat vidyut gaṇa āviddhāḥ ghorāḥ nihrāda kāriṇaḥ anyonya vega abhihatāḥ pravavuḥ sapta mārutāḥ dīpta toya aśanīpātaiḥ vajra vega anala anilaiḥ petuḥ ulkā sahasrāṇi petuḥ ākāśa gāni api arūpavanti rūpāṇi tasmin utpāta lakṣaṇe tamasā niṣprabham sarvam na prājñāyata kiṃcana viveśa rūpiṇī kālī kāla megha avaguṇṭhitā dyauḥ na bhāti abhibhūta arkā ghoreṇa tamasā vṛtā bapuḥ saṃdarśayām āsa divyam kṛṣṇa vapuḥ hariḥ balāhaka añjana nibham balāhaka tanūruham tejasā vapuṣā ca eva kṛṣṇam kṛṣṇam iva acalam dīpta pīta ambara dharam tapta kāñcana bhūṣaṇam dhūma andhakāra vapuṣam yugānta agnim iva utthitam catur dviguṇa pīna aṃsām kirīṭa channa mūrdhajam nandaka ānandita karam śara āśīviṣa dhāriṇam te kṛtāñjalayaḥ sarve devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ mayaśabdam puraskṛtya śaraṇyam śaraṇam gatāḥ sa teṣām tām giram śrutvā viṣṇuḥ dayita daivataḥ manaḥ cakre vināśāya dānavānām mahā mṛdhe bhāsam tu sthitaḥ viṣṇuḥ uttamam vapuḥ āsthitaḥ uvāca devatāḥ sarvāḥ sapratijñam idam vacaḥ śāntim vrajata bhadram vaḥ mā bhaiṣṭa marutām gaṇāḥ mama dānavāḥ sarve trailokyam pratigṛhyatām te tasya satya saṃdhasya viṣṇoḥ vākyena toṣitāḥ devāḥ prītim parām jagmuḥ prāpya iva amṛtam uttamam tatas tamaḥ saṃhriyate vineśuḥ ca balāhakāḥ pravavuḥ ca śivāḥ vātāḥ prasannāḥ ca diśaḥ daśa su prabhāṇi ca jyotiṃṣi candram cakruḥ pradakṣiṇam na vigraham grahāḥ cakruḥ praseduḥ ca api sindhavaḥ virajaskāḥ babhuḥ mārgāḥ nāka mārga ādayaḥ trayaḥ yathārtham ūhuḥ saritaḥ na api cukṣubhire arṇavāḥ āsan śubhāni indriyāṇi narāṇām antarātmasu mahā ṛṣayaḥ vīta śokāḥ vedān uccais adhīyire yajñeṣu ca haviḥ svādu śivam āpa ca pāvakaḥ pravṛtta dharmāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ lokāḥ mudita mānasāḥ uvāca tatas bhayam viṣṇu mayam śrutvā daiteya dānavāḥ kiṃkiṇī jāla nirghoṣam dvīpi carma pariṣkṛtam racitam ratna jālaiḥ ca hema jālaiḥ ca śobhitam mṛga gaṇa ākīrṇam pakṣibhiḥ ca virājitam divya astra tūṇīra dharam payodhara nināditam gadā parigha saṃpūrṇam mūrtimantam iva arṇavam hema keyūra valayam svarṇa kuṇḍala kūbaram dīptam ākāśa gam divyam ratham para ratha arujam atiṣṭhat samara ākāṅkṣī merum dīptaḥ iva aṃśumant tāraḥ tu kroṣa vistāram āyasam vāhayan ratham mahā utkari masaṃkāśam nīlāñjana caya upamam harita loha aṣṭa caraṇam loha īṣā yuga kūbaram loha jālena mahatā sa gavākṣeṇa daṃśitam āyasaiḥ parighaiḥ pūrṇam kṣepaṇīyaiḥ ca mudgaraiḥ prāsaiḥ pāśaiḥ ca vitataiḥ avasaktaiḥ ca mudgaraiḥ śobhitam trāsanīyaiḥ ca tomaraiḥ sa paraśvadhaiḥ pramukhe tasya sainyasya dīpta śṛṅgaḥ iva acalaḥ syandanam vāhayām āsa sapatna anīka mardanam kṣaraḥ tu vikṣaran darpāt netrābhyām roṣa jam jalam sphurat danta oṣṭha vadanaḥ saṃgrāmam saḥ abhyakāṅkṣata tvaṣṭā tu aṣṭādaśa hayam yānam āsthāya dānavaḥ vyūhitaḥ dānavaiḥ vyūhaiḥ paricakrāma vīryavān ṣaṣ sutaḥ śvetaḥ śveta kuṇḍala bhūṣaṇaḥ śveta śaila pratīkāśaḥ yuddhāya abhimukhaḥ sthitaḥ ariṣṭaḥ bali putraḥ tu variṣṭhaḥ adri śilā āyudhaḥ yuddhāya atiṣṭhat āyastaḥ dharādharaḥ iva aparaḥ kiśoraḥ tu ati saṃharṣāt kiśoraḥ iva coditaḥ lambaḥ tu lamba megha ābhaḥ pralamba ambara bhūṣaṇaḥ daitya vyūha gataḥ bhāti sa nīhāraḥ iva aṃśumant svarbhānuḥ āsya yodhī tu daśana oṣṭha īkṣaṇa āyudhaḥ hasan tiṣṭhati daityānām pramukhe sumukhaḥ grahaḥ siṃha vyāghra gatāḥ ca anye varāha ṛkṣa gatāḥ pare kecid khara uṣṭra yātāraḥ kecid toyada vāhanāḥ nānā pakṣi gatāḥ kecid kecid pavana vāhanāḥ tu apare daityāḥ bhīṣaṇāḥ vikṛta ānanāḥ eka pādāḥ dvi pādāḥ ca nanṛtuḥ yuddha kaṅkṣiṇaḥ prakṣveḍamānāḥ bahavaḥ sphoṭayantaḥ ca dānavāḥ dṛpta śārdūla nirghoṣāḥ neduḥ dānava puṃgavāḥ bāhubhiḥ parigha ākāraiḥ tarjayanti sma dānavāḥ prāsaiḥ pāśaiḥ ca khaḍgaiḥ ca tomara aṅkuśa paṭṭisaiḥ cikrīḍuḥ te śataghnībhiḥ śita dhāraiḥ ca mudgaraiḥ gaṇḍaśailaiḥ ca śailaiḥ ca parighaiḥ ca uttama āyudhaiḥ balam raṇa ogha abhyudaya abhyudīrṇam yuyutsayā unmattam iva ābabhāse uvāca surāṇām sarva sainyasya vistaram vaiṣṇavam śṛṇu sa balāḥ sa anugāḥ ca eva saṃnahyanta yathākramam grāmaṇīḥ sarva devānām āruroha sura dvipam dīptimadbhiḥ sadasyaiḥ ca brahmarṣibhiḥ abhiṣṭutaḥ yam ārūḍhaḥ sa bhagavān paryeti maghavān gajam svarge śakra anuyāteṣu deva tūrya anunādiṣu indram samupanṛtyanti śataśas hi apsaraḥ gaṇāḥ ketunā vaṃśa rājena bhrājamānaḥ yathā raviḥ tasthau sura gaṇa anīke daityān nādena bhīṣayan kālapāśān samāvidhya hayaiḥ śaśi kara upamaiḥ vāyu īrita jala udgāraiḥ kurvan līlāḥ sahasraśas pāṇḍura uddhūta vasanaḥ pravāla rucira aṅgadaḥ maṇi śyāma uttama vapūḥ hāra bhāra arpita udaraḥ varuṇaḥ pāśabhṛt madhye deva anīkasya tasthivāḥ yakṣa rākṣasa sainyena guhyakānām gaṇaiḥ api yuktaḥ ca śaṅkha padmābhyām nidhīnām adhipaḥ prabhuḥ rājarāja īśvaraḥ śrīmān gadā pāṇiḥ adṛśyata sa rāja rājaḥ śuśubhe yuddha arthī naravāhanaḥ prekṣamāṇaḥ śivasakhaḥ sākṣāt iva śivaḥ svayam pūrvam pakṣam sahasrākṣaḥ pitṛrājaḥ tu dakṣiṇam varuṇaḥ paścimam pakṣam uttaram naravāhanaḥ caturṣu yuktāḥ catvāraḥ lokapālāḥ bala utkaṭāḥ svām svām diśam rarakṣuḥ te tasya deva balasya ha sūryaḥ sapta aśva yuktena rathena ambara gāminā śriyā jājvalyamānena dīpyamānaiḥ ca raśmibhiḥ cacāra madhye devānām dvādaśātmā dineśvaraḥ somaḥ śveta hayaḥ bhāti syandane śīta raśmivān hima toya prapūrṇābhiḥ bhābhiḥ āplāvayan jagant tam ṛkṣa yoga anugatam śiśirāṃśum dvijeśvaram śaśa chāyā aṅkita tanum naiśasya tamasaḥ kṣayam jyotiṣām īraṇam vyomni rasāṇām rasanam prabhum oṣadhīnām paritrāṇam nidhānam amṛtasya ca jagantaḥ prathamam bhāgam saumyam śaitya mayam rasam dadṛśuḥ dānavāḥ somam hima praharaṇam sthitam yaḥ prāṇaḥ sarva bhūtānām pañcadhā bhidyate nṛṣu yam vadanti uttamam bhūtam yam vadanti aśarīriṇam yam āhuḥ ākāśa gamam śīghra gam śabda yoninam sa vāyuḥ sarva bhūta āyuḥ uddhataḥ svena tejasā sṛjantaḥ sarpa patayaḥ tīvram roṣa mayam viṣam śara bhūtāḥ sura indrāṇām ceruḥ vyātta mukhāḥ divi parvatāḥ tu śilā śṛṅgaiḥ śata śākhaiḥ ca pādapaiḥ upatasthuḥ sura gaṇān prahartum dānavam balam yaḥ sa devaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ padmanābhaḥ trivikramaḥ yuga anta ābhaḥ viśvasya jagantaḥ prabhuḥ bhūmi āpaḥ vyoma bhūta ātmā syāmaḥ śānti karaḥ ari hā sa parīveṣam udyantam savituḥ maṇḍalam yathā savyena ālambya mahatīm sarva asura vināśinīm kareṇa kālīm vapuṣā śatru kāla pradām gadām śeṣaiḥ bhujaiḥ pradīptāni bhujaga ari dhvajaḥ prabhuḥ dadhāra āyudha jātāni śārṅga ādīni mahā yaśāḥ pavana adhika sampātam gagana kṣobhaṇam khagam deva asura vimardeṣu śataśas dṛṣṭa vikramam mahendreṇa amṛtasya arthe vajreṇa kṛta lakṣaṇam śikhinam cūḍinam ca eva tapta kuṇḍala bhūṣaṇam sphīta kroḍa avalambena śītāṃśu sama tejasā pakṣābhyām cāru pattrābhyām āvṛtya divi līlayā yuga ante sa indracāpābhyām toyadābhyām iva ambaram nīla lohita pītābhiḥ patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛtam aruṇāvarajam śrīmān āruroha raṇe hariḥ suparṇaḥ svena vapuṣā suparṇam khecara uttamam tam anvayuḥ deva gaṇāḥ munayaḥ ca samāhitāḥ gīrbhiḥ parama mantrābhiḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca gadādharam tat vaiśravaṇa su śliṣṭam vaivasvata puraḥsaram pavana āviddha nirghoṣam saṃpradīpta hutāśanam viṣṇoḥ jiṣṇoḥ sahiṣṇoḥ ca bhrājiṣṇoḥ tejasā vṛtam uvāca tābhyām balābhyām saṃjajñe tumulaḥ vigrahaḥ tadā surāṇām asurāṇām ca paraspara jaya eṣiṇām dānavāḥ daivataiḥ sārdham nānā praharaṇa udyatāḥ kṣipyamāṇaiḥ ca musalaiḥ saṃpreṣyadbhiḥ ca sāyakaiḥ cāpaiḥ visphāryamāṇaiḥ ca pātyamānaiḥ ca mudgaraiḥ te vadhyamānāḥ balibhiḥ dānavaiḥ jita kāśibhiḥ saṃditāḥ pāśa jālaiḥ ca niryatnāḥ ca śaraiḥ kṛtāḥ praviṣṭāḥ dānavām māyām na śekuḥ te viceṣṭitum tat stambhitam iva ābhāti niṣprāṇa sadṛśa ākṛti balam surāṇām asuraiḥ niṣprayatna āyudham kṛtam māyā pāśān vikarṣan ca chindan vajreṇa tān śarān te anyonyam na avabudhyanta devān vā vāhanāni vā ghoreṇa tamasā āviṣṭāḥ puruhūtasya tejasā māyā pāśaiḥ vimuktāḥ tu yatnavantaḥ sura uttamāḥ vapūṃṣi daitya saṃghānām tamaḥ bhūtāni apātayan apadhvastāḥ visaṃjñāḥ ca tamasā nīla varcasaḥ petuḥ te dānava gaṇāḥ chinna pakṣāḥ iva acalāḥ tadā sṛjat mahā māyām mayaḥ tām tāmasīm dahan yuga anta uddyota jananīm sṛṣṭām aurveṇa vahninā sā dadāha tamaḥ sarvam māyā maya vikalpitā daityāḥ ca āditya vapuṣaḥ sadyas uttasthuḥ āhave māyām aurvīm samāsādya dahyamānāḥ divaukasaḥ bhejire candra viṣayam śītāṃśu salila hradam te dahyamānāḥ aurveṇa tejasā bhraṣṭa tejasaḥ śaśaṃsuḥ vajriṇe devāḥ saṃtaptāḥ śaraṇa eṣiṇaḥ saṃtapte māyayā sainye dahyamāne ca dānavaiḥ brahmarṣi jaḥ śakra tapaḥ tepe su dāruṇam aurvaḥ pūrvam sa tejasvī sadṛśaḥ brahmaṇaḥ guṇaiḥ hiraṇyakaśipuḥ ca eva dānavaḥ dāvaneśvaraḥ ṛṣim vijñāpayām āsa purā parama tejasam bhagavan chinna mūlam idam kulam kaumāram vratam āsthāya kleśam eva anuvartase bahūni vipra gotrāṇi munīnām bhāvitātmanām eka dehāni tiṣṭhanti viviktāni vinā prajāḥ dharatsu utsanna bhūteṣu teṣu te na asti kāraṇam bhavān tu tapasā śreṣṭhaḥ prajāpati sama dyutiḥ tat pravartasva vaṃśāya vardhaya ātmānam ātmanā jagarhe tān ṛṣi gaṇān vacanam ca idam abravīt yathā ayam śāśvataḥ dharmaḥ munīnām vihitaḥ purā ārṣam vai sevatām karma vanya mūla phala āśinaḥ dvijānām vṛttayaḥ tisraḥ ye gṛha āśrama vāsinaḥ asmākam tu vanam vṛttiḥ vanya āśrama nivāsinām abbhakṣāḥ vāyubhakṣāḥ ca dantolūkhalinaḥ tathā aśmakuṭṭāḥ daśa tapāḥ pañca sapta tapāḥ ca ye brahmacaryāt brāhmaṇasya brāhmaṇa tvam vidhīyate ye sthitāḥ brahmacaryeṇa brāhmaṇāḥ divi te sthitāḥ na asti yogam vinā siddhiḥ na asti siddhim vinā yaśaḥ na asti loke yaśaḥ mūlam brahmacaryāt param tapaḥ yaḥ nigṛhya indriya grāmam bhūta grāmam ca pañcakam kva dārāḥ kva ca saṃyogaḥ kva ca bhāva viparyayaḥ yat iyam brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā manasā mānasī prajā yadi asti tapasaḥ vīryam yuṣmākam amita ātmanām sṛjadhvam mānasān putrān prājāpatyena karmaṇā manasā nirmitā yoniḥ ādhātavyā tapasvinā na dāra yogam bījam vā vratam uktam tapasvinām vapuḥ dīpta antarātmānam eṣa kṛtvā manaḥ mayam dāra yogam vinā srakṣye putram ātma tanūruham evam ātmānam ātmā me dvitīyam janayiṣyati ūrvaḥ tu tapasā āviṣṭaḥ niveśya ūrum hutāśane tasya ūrum sahasā bhittvā jvālā mālī nirindhanaḥ jagantaḥ dahana ākāṅkṣī putraḥ agniḥ samapadyata didhakṣan iva lokān trīn jajñe parama kopanaḥ utpanna mātraḥ ca uvāca pitaram dīptayā girā tridiva ārohibhiḥ jvālaiḥ jṛmbhamāṇaḥ diśaḥ daśa putra idam dhāryatām tejaḥ lokānām kriyatām dayā vāsam ca asya pradāsyāmi prāśanam ca amṛta upamam tathyam etat mama vacaḥ śṛṇu tvam vadatām vara uvāca dhanyaḥ asmi anugṛhītaḥ asmi yat me adya bhagavān śiśoḥ matim etām dadāti iha parama anugrahāya vai prabhāta kāle saṃprāpte kāṅkṣitavye samāgame tatra aham āse nirataḥ piban vāri mayam havaiḥ tatas yuga ante bhūtānām eṣa ca aham ca suvrata sahitau vicariṣyāvaḥ niṣprāṇana karau iha eṣaḥ agniḥ antakālasya salila āśī mayā kṛtaḥ dahanaḥ sarva bhūtānām sa deva asura rakṣasām evam astu iti saḥ api agniḥ saṃvṛta jvāla maṇḍalaḥ aurvasya agneḥ prabhāva jñāḥ svām svām gatim upāśritāḥ hiraṇyakaśipuḥ dṛṣṭvā tat adbhutam apūjayat aurvam praṇata sarva aṅgaḥ vākyam ca idam uvāca ha tapasā te muni śreṣṭha parituṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ tam mā paśya samāpannam tava eva ārādhane ratam yat sīdeyam muni śreṣṭha tava eva syāt parājayaḥ uvāca imām ca māyām gṛhṇīṣva mama putreṇa nirmitām nirindhanām agni mayām duḥsparśām pāvakaiḥ api eṣā te svasya vaṃśasya vaśagā ari vinigrahe rakṣiṣyati ātma pakṣam ca parān ca pradahiṣyati sā eṣā durviṣahā māyā devaiḥ api durāsadā aurveṇa nirmitā pūrvam pāvakena ūrva sūnunā tasmin tu vyutthite daitye nirvīya eṣā na saṃśayaḥ śāpaḥ hi asyāḥ purā dattaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ yena eva tejasā dīyatām me sakhiḥ śakra toya yoniḥ niśākaraḥ māyām etām haniṣyāmi tvad prasādāt na saṃśayaḥ uvāca evam astu iti saṃhṛṣṭaḥ śakraḥ tridaśa vardhanaḥ saṃdideśa agratas somam yuddhāya śiśirāyudham asurāṇām vināśāya jaya artham ca divaukasām tvam apratima vīryaḥ ca jyotiṣām ca īśvara īśvaraḥ tvad mayam sarva lokānām rasam rasa vidaḥ viduḥ kṣaya vṛddhiḥ tava vyaktā sāgare khe ca maṇḍale loka chāyā mayam lakṣma te aṅke śaśa saṃsthitam tvam āditya pathāt ūrdhvam jyotiṣām ca upari sthitaḥ śveta bhānuḥ hima tanuḥ jyotiṣām adhipaḥ śaśī abda kṛt kāla yoga ātmā yajña rasaḥ avyayaḥ śītāṃśuḥ amṛta ādhāraḥ capalaḥ śveta vāhanaḥ tvam kāntiḥ kānta vapuṣām tvam somaḥ soma vṛttinām saumyaḥ tvam sarva bhūtānām timira ghnaḥ tvam ṛkṣa rāj śamayasva āsurīm māyām yayā dahyāma saṃyuge eṣa varṣāmi śiśiram daitya māyā apakarṣaṇam etān mad śīta nirdagdhān paśyasva hima veṣṭitān vimāyān vimadān ca eva daitya saṃghān mahā āhave tatas himakara utsṛṣṭāḥ sa bāṣpāḥ hima vṛṣṭayaḥ megha gaṇāḥ iva tau pāśa śukla aṃśu dharau varuṇa indū mahā raṇe jaghnatuḥ hima pātaiḥ ca pāśa pātaiḥ ca dānavān tābhyām āplāvitam sainyam tat dānavam adṛśyata tau udyata aṃśu pāśau tu śaśāṅka varuṇau ubhau tām māyām āstām devau daiteya nirmitām śītāṃśu jala nirdagdhāḥ pāśaiḥ ca prasitāḥ mṛdhe na śekuḥ calitum daityāḥ viśiraskāḥ iva adrayaḥ śītāṃśu nihatāḥ te tu petuḥ daityāḥ hima arditāḥ hima plāvita sarva aṅgāḥ niruṣmāṇaḥ iva agrayaḥ teṣām tu divi daityānām viparīta prabhāni ha tān pāśa hasta grathitān chāditān śītaraśmibhiḥ mayaḥ dadarśa māyāvī dānavān divi dānavaḥ sa śilā jāla vitatām gaṇḍaśaila aṭṭahāsinīm pādapa utkaṭa kūṭa agrām kandara ākīrṇa kānanām siṃha vyāghra gaja ākīrṇām nadatīm dvipa yūthapaiḥ mṛga gaṇa ākīrṇām pavana āghūrṇita drumām nirmitām svena putreṇa krauñcena divi kāmagām prathitām pārvatīm māyām sasṛje sa samantataḥ sa aśma śabdaiḥ śilā varṣaiḥ prapatadbhiḥ ca pādapaiḥ nijaghne deva saṃghān tān dānavān ca api ajīvayat naiśākarī vāruṇī ca māye antardadhatuḥ tatas aśmabhiḥ ca āyasa ghanaiḥ kirat deva gaṇān raṇe sa aśma saṃghāta viṣamā druma parvata saṃkaṭā na an āhataḥ aśmabhiḥ kaścid śilābhiḥ ca api a tāḍitaḥ niṣprayatnam sura anīkam varjayitvā gadādharam sa hi yuddha gataḥ śrīmān īśaḥ na sma vyakampata sahiṣṇu tvāt jagatsvāmī na cukrodha gadādharaḥ kāla jñaḥ kāla megha ābhaḥ samīkṣan kālam āhave deva asura vimardam sa draṣṭu kāmaḥ janārdanaḥ tatas bhagavantā ādiṣṭau raṇe pāvaka mārutau coditau viṣṇu vākyena tau māyām apakarṣatām tābhyām udbhrānta meghābhyām pravṛddhābhyām mahā mṛdhe dagdhā sā pārvatī māyā bhasma bhūtā nanāśa ha saḥ analaḥ anila saṃyuktaḥ saḥ anilaḥ ca anala ākulaḥ vāyuḥ pradhāvitaḥ tatra paścāt agniḥ ca mārutāt ceratuḥ dānava anīke krīḍantau anila analau dānavānām vimāneṣu vimāneṣu samantataḥ vātaskandha apaviddheṣu kṛta karmaṇi pāvake māyā vadhe vinirvṛtte stūyamāne gadādhare saṃprahṛṣṭeṣu deveṣu sādhu sādhu iti sarvaśas prakṛti stheṣu lokeṣu nṛṣu cāritra bandhuṣu yajña śobhiṣu deveṣu svarga artham darśayatsu ca lokapāleṣu sarveṣu dikṣu saṃyāna vartiṣu bhāve tapasi śuddhānām abhāve pāpa karmaṇām prajā rakṣaṇa yukteṣu bhrājamāneṣu rājsu praśānta kalmaṣe loke śānte tamasi dāruṇe tad mayāḥ vimalāḥ lokāḥ tābhyām jaya kṛta kriyāḥ pūrvadeva bhayam śrutvā māruta agni bhayam mahat kālanemiḥ iti khyātaḥ dānavaḥ pratyadṛśyata bhāskara ākāra mukuṭaḥ śiñjita ābharaṇa aṅgadaḥ mandara utkīrṇa saṃkāśaḥ mahārajata saṃvṛtaḥ śata praharaṇa udagraḥ śata bāhuḥ śata ānanaḥ śata śīrṣaḥ sthitaḥ śrīmān śataśṛṅgaḥ iva acalaḥ kakṣe mahati saṃvṛddhaḥ nidāghaḥ iva pāvakaḥ dhūmra keśaḥ hari śmaśruḥ daṃṣṭra āla oṣṭha puṭa ānanaḥ mukha niḥśvāsaiḥ vṛṣṭimantaḥ balāhakān didhakṣantam iva āyāntam sarvān deva gaṇān mṛdhe tarjayantam sura gaṇān chādayantam diśaḥ daśa saṃvarta kāle tṛṣitam dṛptam mṛtyum iva utthitam lamba ābharaṇa pūrṇena kiṃcid calita varmaṇā tam kālanemim samare dviṣatām kāla saṃmitam tam sma vīkṣanti bhūtāni kramantam kālaneminam saḥ ucchrayan prathamam pādam māruta āghūrṇita ambaram dṛṣṭvā kālam iva āyāntam kālanemim bhaya āvaham uvāca dānavānām tu piprīṣuḥ kālanemiḥ sa dānavaḥ tam trailoya antara gatam dṛṣṭvā te dānava īśvarāḥ uttasthuḥ apariśrāntāḥ prāpya iva amṛtam uttamam te vīta bhaya saṃtrāsāḥ maya tāra purogamāḥ rejuḥ āyodhana gatāḥ dānavāḥ yuddha kaṅkṣiṇaḥ mantram abhyasyatam teṣām vyūham ca paridhāvatām prekṣatām ca abhavat prītiḥ dānavam kālaneminam te api sarve bhayam tyaktvā hṛṣṭāḥ yoddhum upasthitāḥ mayaḥ tāraḥ varāhaḥ ca hayagrīvaḥ ca vīryavān ariṣṭaḥ bali putraḥ ca tathā eva ca dānavāḥ kṛtinaḥ jagmuḥ kālaneminam uttamam te gadābhiḥ ca gurvībhiḥ cakraiḥ ca sa paraśu aghaiḥ kāla kalpaiḥ ca musalaiḥ kṣepaṇīyaiḥ ca mudgaraiḥ aśmabhiḥ ca aṭṭa sadṛśaiḥ gaṇḍaśailaiḥ ca daṃśitaiḥ paṭṭisaiḥ bhindipālaiḥ ca parighaiḥ ca uttama āyasaiḥ ghātanībhiḥ ca gurvībhiḥ śataghnībhiḥ tathā eva ca dorbhiḥ ca āyata pīnābhiḥ prāsaiḥ pāśaiḥ ca mudgaraiḥ vajraiḥ praharaṇīyaiḥ ca dīpyadbhiḥ ca api tomaraiḥ vikośaiḥ ca asibhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ śūlaiḥ ca śita nirmalaiḥ te vai saṃdīpta manasaḥ pragṛhīta uttama āyudhāḥ puraskṛtya tasthuḥ saṃgrāma mūrdhani sā dīpta śastra pravarā daityānām śuśubhe camūḥ dyauḥ nimīlita nakṣatrā ghana nīla ambuda āgame devatānām api camūḥ mumude śakra pālitā dīptā śīta uṣṇa tejobhyām candra bhāskara tejasā vāyu vegavatī saumyā tārā gaṇa patākinī saṃpradīpta agni pavanā nārāyaṇa parāyaṇā sā samudra ogha sadṛśī divyā deva mahā camūḥ rarāja astravatī bhīmā yakṣa gandharva śālinī tayoḥ camvoḥ tadānīm tu babhūva sa samāgamaḥ saṃyogaḥ yathā syāt yuga paryaye niścakramuḥ balābhyām tu tābhyām bhīmāḥ sura asurāḥ pūrva aparābhyām saṃrabdhāḥ sāgarābhyām iva ambudāḥ tābhyām balābhyām saṃhṛṣṭāḥ ceruḥ te deva dānavāḥ vanābhyām pārvatīyābhyām puṣpitābhyām yathā gajāḥ samājaghnuḥ tatas bherīḥ śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ ca na ekaśas sa dyām divam bhuvam ca eva diśaḥ ca samapūrayat jyā ghāta tala nirghoṣaḥ dhanuṣām kūjitāni ca devatāḥ tu aśanīḥ ghorāḥ parighān ca uttama āyasān sasarjuḥ ājau nistriṃśān gadāḥ gurvīḥ ca dānavāḥ gadā nipātaiḥ bhagna aṅgāḥ bāṇaiḥ ca śakalīkṛtāḥ tatas rathaiḥ sa turagaiḥ vimānaiḥ ca āśu gāmibhiḥ samīyuḥ te su saṃrabdhāḥ roṣāt anyonyam āhave teṣām rathānām tumulaḥ sa śabdaḥ śabda vāhinām saṃbādham eke saṃprāpya na śekuḥ calitum rathāḥ saṃhrāda māna ābharaṇāḥ jaghnuḥ tatra asi carmiṇaḥ kṣarat jalānām sadṛśāḥ jaladānām samāgame deva dānava saṃkṣubdham saṃkulam yuddham ābabhau tasya vidyut cala āpīḍāḥ pradīpta aśani varṣiṇaḥ gātrāt nāgaśiraḥ prakhyāḥ viniṣpetuḥ balāhakāḥ krodhāt niḥśvasataḥ tasya bhrū bheda sveda varṣiṇaḥ sa agni niṣpeṣa pavanāḥ mukhāt niśceruḥ arciṣaḥ pañca āsyāḥ kṛṣṇa vapuṣaḥ lelihantaḥ iva uragāḥ saṃdhyā ātapa grasta śikhaḥ sākṣāt meruḥ iva acalaḥ ūru vega pratikṣiptaiḥ śaila śṛṅga agra pādapaiḥ apātayat deva gaṇān vajreṇa iva mahā girīn na śekuḥ calitum devāḥ kālanemi hatāḥ yudhi muṣṭibhiḥ nihatāḥ kecid kecid hi vidalīkṛtāḥ tena vitrāsitāḥ devāḥ samare kālaneminā tena śakraḥ sahasrākṣaḥ saṃditaḥ śara bandhanaiḥ airāvata gataḥ saṃkhye calitum na śaśāka ha nirjala ambhoda sadṛśaḥ nirjala arṇava saprabhaḥ nirvyāpāraḥ kṛtaḥ tena vipāśaḥ varuṇaḥ mṛdhe raṇe vaiśravaṇaḥ tena parighaiḥ kāmarūpibhiḥ yāmyām avasthām amaraḥ nītaḥ svām diśam āviśat sa lokapālān utsādya hṛtvā teṣām ca karma tat dikṣu sarvāsu deham svam caturdhā vidadhe tadā mahāra lakṣmīm somasya tam ca asya viṣayam mahat cālayāmāsa dīpta aṃśum svargadvārāt sa bhāskaram sa ayanam ca asya viṣayam jahāra dinakarma ca saḥ agnim deva mukhe dṛṣṭvā cakāra ātma mukheśayam vāyum ca tarasā jitvā cakāra ātma vaśa anugam sa samudrān samānīya sarvāḥ ca saritaḥ balāt cakāra ātma vaśe vīryāt deha bhūtāḥ ca sindhavaḥ apaḥ sa vaśa gāḥ kṛtvā divijātāḥ ca bhūmijāḥ sthāpayām āsa jagatīm su guptām dharaṇīdharaiḥ sa svayaṃbhūḥ iva ābhāti mahā bhūta patiḥ mahān pāvaka anila saṃghātaḥ rarāja yudhi dānavaḥ pārameṣṭhye sthitaḥ sthāne lokānām prabhava apyaye tam tuṣṭuvuḥ daitya gaṇāḥ devāḥ iva pitāmaham uvāca pañca tam na abhyavartanta viparītena karmaṇā vedaḥ dharmaḥ kṣamā satyam śrīḥ ca nārāyaṇa āśrayā sa teṣām anupasthānāt sa krodhaḥ dānava īśvaraḥ yayau dānavānām vināśāya bhrāmayantam gadām śubhām sa jala ambhoda sadṛśam vidyut sadṛśa vāsasam su ārūḍham svarṇa pattra āḍhyam śikhinam kāśyapam khagam dṛṣṭvā daitya vināśāya raṇe svastham avasthitam dānavaḥ viṣṇum akṣobhyam babhāṣe kṣubdha mānasaḥ ayam sa ripuḥ asmākam pūrveṣām dānava ṛṣiṇām yena naḥ saṃyugeṣu adya bahavaḥ dānavāḥ hatāḥ ayam sa nirghṛṇaḥ yuddhe strī bāla nirapatrapaḥ yena dānava nārīṇām sīmanta uddharaṇam kṛtam ayam sa viṣṇuḥ devānām vaikuṇṭhaḥ ca divaukasām ayam sa nāthaḥ devānām asmābhiḥ viprakṛṣyatām asya krodham samāsādya hiraṇyakaśipuḥ hataḥ asya chāyām samāśritya devāḥ makha mukhe sthitāḥ ayam sa nidhane hetuḥ sarveṣām daitavat viṣām asya cakram praviṣṭāni kulāni asmākam āhave savituḥ tejasā tulyam cakram kṣipati śatruṣu ayam sa kālaḥ daityānām kāla bhūte mayi sthite diṣṭyā idānīm samakṣam mama viṣṇuḥ eṣa samāgataḥ adya mad bāṇa niṣpiṣṭaḥ mayi eva praṇamiṣyati yāsyāmi apacitim diṣṭyā pūrveṣām adya saṃyuge imam nārāyaṇam hatvā dānavānām bhaya āvaham kṣipram eva vadhiṣyāmi raṇe nārāyaṇam śairaiḥ bādhati eṣaḥ antakaḥ purā bhūtvā padmanābhaḥ iti smṛtaḥ dvidhā bhūtam vapuḥ kṛtvā siṃha ardham nara saṃsthitam pitaram mama jaghāna ekaḥ hiraṇyakaśipum purā trīn lokān ca jahāra eṣa kramamāṇaḥ tribhiḥ kramaiḥ bhūyas tu idānīm samare saṃprāpte tārakāmaye saḥ evam uktvā bahudhā kṣipan nārāyaṇam raṇe kṣipyamāṇaḥ asura indreṇa yaḥ cukopa gadādharaḥ kṣamā balena manasā sa smitam vākyam abravīt hataḥ tvam darpa jaiḥ doṣaiḥ kṣamām yaḥ atītya bhāṣase aham tvām daitya paśyāmi pūrvāṇām mārga gāminam adya tvām nāśayiṣyāmi deva vyāghāta kāriṇam sveṣu sveṣu ca sthāneṣu sthāpayiṣyāmi devatāḥ evam bruvati vākyam tu mṛdhe śrīvatsa dhāriṇi jahāsa dānavaḥ krodhāt hastān cakre ca sa āyudhān sa bāhu śatam udyamya sarva astra grahaṇam raṇe krodhāt rudhira rakta akṣaḥ viṣṇoḥ vakṣasi atāḍayat dānavāḥ ca api samare maya tāra purogamāḥ udyata āyudha nistriṃśāḥ sarve viṣṇum abhidravan saṃsaktaḥ ca suparṇena kālanemiḥ mahā asuraḥ sarva prāṇena mahatīm gadām udyamya bāhubhiḥ mumoca jvalitām ghorām saṃrabdhaḥ garuḍa upari suparṇam vyathitam dṛṣṭvā kṣatam ca vapuḥ ātmanaḥ sa diśaḥ pradiśaḥ ca eva kham ca gām ca eva pūrayan tam jayāya sura indrāṇām vardhamānam nabhastale padbhyām ākramya vasudhām diśaḥ pracchādya bāhubhiḥ dīpta agni sadṛśam ghoram darśanīyam su darśanam advitīyam prahāreṣu kṣura paryanta maṇḍalam sraj dāma mālā vitatam kāma gam kāmarūpiṇam svayam svayambhunā sṛṣṭam bhaya dam sarva vidviṣām mahā ṛṣi roṣaiḥ āviṣṭam nityam āhava darpitam tasmāt yasya muhyanti lokāḥ sa sthāṇu jaṅgamāḥ kravyādāni ca bhūtāni tṛptim yānti mahā mṛdhe tam apratima karmāṇam samānam sūrya varcasā saṃmuṣṇan dānavam tejaḥ samare svena tejasā ciccheda bāhūn cakreṇa śrīdharaḥ kālanemeḥ tat ca vaktra śatam ghoram sa agni cūrṇa aṭṭahāsi yat sa chinna bāhuḥ viśirāḥ na prākampata dānavaḥ kabandha avasthitaḥ saṃkhye viśākhaḥ iva pādapaḥ tam vitatya mahā pakṣau vāyoḥ kṛtvā samam javam urasā pātayām āsa garuḍaḥ kālaneminam tasmin nipatite daitye devāḥ sa ṛṣi gaṇāḥ tadā sādhu sādhu iti vaikuṇṭham sametāḥ pratyapūjayan apare ye tu daityāḥ vai yuddhe dṛṣṭa parākramāḥ te sarve bāhubhiḥ vyāptāḥ na śekuḥ calitum raṇe kāṃścid keśeṣu jagrāha kāṃścid kaṇṭhe nyapīḍayat pāṭayan kasyacid vaktram madhye kāṃścid agṛhyata nipetuḥ teṣu sarveṣu daityeṣu hateṣu puruṣottamaḥ tasthau śakra priyam kṛtvā kṛta karmā gadādharaḥ tam deśam ājagāma āśu brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ sarvaiḥ brahmarṣibhiḥ sārdham gandharvaiḥ sa apsaraḥ gaṇaiḥ kṛtam deva mahat karma surāṇām śalyam uddhṛtam vadhena anena daityānām vayam ca paritoṣitāḥ yaḥ ayam tvayā hataḥ viṣṇo kālanemiḥ mahā asuraḥ eṣa devān paribhavan lokān ca sa carācarān ṛṣīṇām kadanam kṛtvā mām api pratigarjati yat ayam kāla tulya ābhaḥ kālanemiḥ nipātitaḥ brahmarṣayaḥ tvām tatrasthāḥ pratīkṣante sadaḥ gatāḥ kim ca aham tava dāsyāmi varam vara bhṛtām vara sureṣu api sa daityeṣu varāṇām vara daḥ bhavān asmin eva mṛdhe viṣṇo śakrāya su mahātmane evam uktaḥ bhagavatā brahmanā hariḥ īśvaraḥ devān śakra mukhān sarvān uvāca śubhayā girā śrūyatām tridaśāḥ sarve yāvantaḥ stha samāgatāḥ dānavāḥ vikrama upetāḥ śakrāt api mahattarāḥ tat iṣṭām bhajatām śakraḥ diśam varuṇaḥ eva ca yāmyām yamaḥ pālayatām uttarām ca dhanādhipaḥ ṛkṣaiḥ saha yathāyogam kālam caratu candramāḥ abdam hi ṛtu mukham sūryaḥ bhajatām ayanaiḥ saha mā ājyabhāgāḥ pravartantām sadasyaiḥ abhipūjitāḥ hūyantām agnayaḥ vipraiḥ veda dṛṣṭena karmaṇā devāḥ ca bali homena svādhyāyena mahā ṛṣayaḥ śrāddhena pitaraḥ ca eva tṛptim yāntu yathāsukham vāyuḥ caratu mārga sthaḥ tridhā dīpyatu pāvakaḥ trayaḥ varṇāḥ ca lokān trīn tarpayantu ātma jaiḥ guṇaiḥ yajñavaḥ saṃpravartantām dīkṣaṇīyaiḥ dvijātibhiḥ dakṣiṇāḥ ca api vartantām yathoktam sarva satriṇām ca ca ca ca trailokya mātaraḥ sarvāḥ sāgaram yāntu nimnagāḥ daityebhyaḥ tyajyatām bhītiḥ śāntim vrajata devatāḥ sva gṛhe svarga loke vā saṃgrāme vā viśeṣataḥ saumyānām ṛju bhāvānām bhavatām ca ārjavā matiḥ evam uktvā sura gaṇān viṣṇuḥ satya parākramaḥ jagāma brahmaṇā sārdham brahma lokam mahā yaśāḥ etat āścaryam abhavat saṃgrāme tārakā maye dānavānām ca viṣṇoḥ ca yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi brahma loke ca kim sthānam kam vā yogam upāsta saḥ kam vā dadhāra niyamam sa vibhuḥ bhūtabhāvanaḥ śriyam āpnoti vipulām sura asura nara arcitām uvāca śṛṇu nārāyaṇasya ādau vistareṇa pravṛttayaḥ brahma lokam yathā ārūḍhaḥ brahmaṇā saha modate kāmam tasya gatiḥ sūkṣmā devaiḥ api durānugā yat tu śakṣyāmi aham vaktum tat me nigadataḥ śṛṇu agnīṣoma mayam lokam yam viduḥ viduṣaḥ janāḥ tam somam agnim lokam ca veda viṣṇum pitāmahaḥ mathyamāneṣu bhūteṣu tathā lokaḥ janārdanāt yathā bhūta indriya avāptiḥ vihitā bhuvi dehinām tathā prāṇeśvara avāptiḥ devānām divi vaiṣṇavā sattriṇām sattra phala daḥ pavitram parama ātmavān asya pāram na paśyanti bahavaḥ pāratantriṇaḥ eṣa pāram param ca eva lokānām veda mādhavaḥ śṛṇu vai yat tadā vṛttam brahma loke purātanam sa gatvā brahmaṇaḥ lokam dṛṣṭvā paitāmaham padam vavande tān ṛṣīn sarvān viṣṇuḥ ārṣeṇa karmaṇā saḥ agnim prāk savane dṛṣṭvā hūyamānam mahā ṛṣibhiḥ avandata mahā tejāḥ kṛtvā paurvāhṇikam vidhim sa dadarśa makheṣu ājyaiḥ ijyamānam mahā ṛṣibhiḥ bhāgam yajñiyam aśnānam sva deham aparam sthitam abhivādya abhivādyānām ṛṣīṇām brahmavarcasām sa dadarśa ucchritān yūpān caṣāla agra vibhūṣitān makheṣu ca brahmarṣibhiḥ śataśas kṛta lakṣaṇān jya dhūmam samāghrāya śṛṇvan vedān dvija īritān tam ūcuḥ ṛṣayaḥ devāḥ sadasyāḥ sadasi sthitāḥ svāgatam te suraśreṣṭha padmanābha mahā dyute idam yajñiyam ātithyam mantrataḥ pratigṛhyatām tvam asya yajña pūtasya pātram pādyasya pāvanaḥ atithiḥ tvam hi mantra uktaḥ sa dṛṣṭaḥ satatam mataḥ yadi ātmānam iha asmābhiḥ ijyamānam nirīkṣase uvāca ṛṣibhiḥ pūjitaḥ taiḥ tu viveśa hariḥ īśvaraḥ paurāṇam brahma sadanam divyam nārāyaṇa āśramam sa tatra viviśe hṛṣṭaḥ tān āmantrya sadaḥ gatān svena nāmnā parijñātam sa tam nārāyaṇa āśramam su adhiṣṭhitam bhūta gaṇaiḥ śāśvataiḥ ca mahā ṛṣibhiḥ vapuṣā padmanābhasya sa deśaḥ tejasā vṛtaḥ sa sahasra śirāḥ bhūtvā śayanāya upacakrame lokānām anta kāla jñā kālī nayana śālinī upatasthe mahātmānam nidrā tam kāla rūpiṇī sa śiśye śayane divye samudra ambhoda śītale tam śayānam mahātmānam bhavāya jagantaḥ prabhum upāsām cakrire viṣṇum devāḥ sa ṛṣi gaṇāḥ tadā ādyasya sadanam padmam brahmaṇaḥ sūrya saṃnibham āvartayati lokānām sarveṣām kāla paryayam vivṛtāt tasya vadanāt niḥśvāsa pavana īritāḥ te sṛṣṭāḥ prāṇinām oghāḥ vibhaktāḥ brahmaṇā svayam caturdhā svām gatim jagmuḥ kṛtānta uktena karmaṇā na tam veda svayam brahmā na api brahmarṣayaḥ avyayāḥ viṣṇum nidrā mayam yogam praviṣṭam tamasā āvṛtam yaḥ atra kaḥ śete kaḥ śvasan kaḥ ca na iṅgate kaḥ bhogavān kaḥ dyutimān kṛṣṇāt kṛṣṇataraḥ ca kaḥ na ca enam śekuḥ anveṣṭum karmataḥ janmataḥ api vā purāṇam tam purāṇeṣu ṛṣayaḥ saṃpracakṣate śrūyate ca asya caritam deveṣu api purātanam mahā purāṇāt prabhṛti param tasya na vidyate tena imāḥ śrutayaḥ vyāptāḥ vaidikāḥ laukikāḥ ca yāḥ bhava kāle bhavati eṣa lokānām bhūta bhāvanaḥ dānavānām abhāvāya jāgarti madhusūdanaḥ yadā enam vīkṣitum devāḥ na śekuḥ suptam acyutam śarad pravṛtta yajñaḥ hi jāgarti madhusūdanaḥ tat idam vārṣikam cakram kārayati ambuda īśvaraḥ vaiṣṇavam karma kurvāṇaḥ supte viṣṇau puraṃdaraḥ yā hi eṣā gahvarī māyā nidrā iti jaganti sthitā akasmāt dveṣiṇī ghorā kālarātriḥ mahīkṣitām asyāḥ tanuḥ tamaḥ dvārā niśā divasa nāśinī jīvita ardha harā ghorā sarva prāṇabhṛtām bhuvi na etayā kaścid āviṣṭaḥ jṛmbhamāṇaḥ muhur muhur śaktaḥ prasahitum vegam majjan iva mahā arṇave anna jāḥ bhuvi martyānām śrama jāḥ vā kathaṃcana svapna ante kṣīyate hi eṣā prāyaśas bhuvi dehinām mṛtyu kāle ca bhūtānām prāṇān nāśayate bhṛśam deveṣu api dadhāra enām na anyaḥ nārāyaṇāt ṛte sakhī sarva harasya eṣā māyā viṣṇu śarīra jā sā eṣā nārāyaṇa mukhe dṛṣṭā kamala locanā evam eṣā hita arthāya lokānām kṛṣṇavartmanā sa tayā nidrayā channaḥ tasmin nārāyaṇa āśrame śete sma hi tadā viṣṇuḥ mohayan jagant avyayaḥ tasya varṣa sahasrāṇi śayānasya mahātmanaḥ sa tu dvāpara paryante dṛṣṭvā lokān su duḥkhitān prābudhyata mahā tejāḥ stūyamānaḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ ūcuḥ jahīhi nidrām sahajām bhukta pūrvām iva srajam ime te brahmaṇā sārdham devāḥ darśana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ ime tvām brahma viduṣaḥ brahma saṃstava vādinaḥ vardhayanti hṛṣīkeśe ṛṣayaḥ saṃśita vratāḥ eteṣām ātma bhūtānām bhūtānām bhūta bhāvana śṛṇu viṣṇo śubhām vācam bhū vyoma agni anila ambhasām ime tvā sapta munayaḥ sahitāḥ muni maṇḍalaiḥ uttiṣṭha śatapattra akṣa padmanābha mahā dyute kāraṇam kiṃcid utpannam devānām kārya gauravāt uvāca udatiṣṭhat dhṛṣīkeśaḥ śriyā paramayā jvalan sa dadarśa surān sarvān sametān sa pitāmahān mad arthe samāgatān tān uvāca hariḥ devān nidrā viśrānta locanaḥ tattva dṛṣṭārthayā vācā dharma hetu artha yuktayā kasya vā kena vā kāryam kim vā mayi na vartate nṛṇām āyāsa jananam śīghram icchāmi veditum śivāya bhavatām arthe sthitaḥ kim karavāṇi vaḥ uvāca tat śrutvā viṣṇu gaditam brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ uvāca paramam vākyam hitam sarva divaukasām na asti kiṃcid bhayam viṣṇo surāṇām asura antaka yeṣām bhavān abhaya daḥ karṇadhāraḥ raṇe raṇe dharme prayatamānānām mānavānām kutas bhayam na akāla dharmaṇā mṛtyuḥ śaknoti prasamīkṣitum mānavānām ca patayaḥ pārthivāḥ ca parasparam mithas te prajānām śubha karāḥ kara daiḥ avigarhitāḥ akaraiḥ viprayukta arthāḥ kośam āpūrayan sadā sphītān janapadān svān svān pālayantaḥ kṣamā pare atīkṣṇat aṇḍāḥ caturaḥ varṇān jugupuḥ añjasā na udvejanīyāḥ bhūtānām sacivaiḥ sādhu pūjitāḥ catur aṅga balaiḥ yuktāḥ ṣaḍguṇān upayuñjate dhanurveda pare sarve sarve vedeṣu niṣṭhitāḥ yajanti ca yathākālam yajñaiḥ vipula dakṣiṇaiḥ vedān adhītya dīkṣābhiḥ mahā ṛṣīn brahmacaryayā śrāddhaiḥ ca medhyaiḥ śataśas tarpayanti pitāmahān te parāvara dṛṣṭa arthāḥ mahā ṛṣi sama tejasaḥ bhūyas kṛta yugam kartum utsahante narādhipāḥ teṣām eva prabhāvena śivam varṣati vāsavaḥ yathārtham ca vavuḥ vātāḥ virajaskāḥ diśaḥ daśa nirutpātā ca vasudhā su pracārāḥ ca vai grahāḥ havyaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ tṛptaḥ śubha gandhaḥ hutāśanaḥ evam samyak pravṛtteṣu nivṛtteṣu aparādhāt tarpayatsu mahīm kṛtsnām nṝṇām kāla bhayam kutas teṣām jvalita kīrtīnām anyonyam anuvartinām rājñām balaiḥ balavatām pīḍyate vasudhā talam sā iyam bhāra pariśrāntā pīḍyamānā narādhipaiḥ pṛthivī samanuprāptā nauḥ iva āsan aviplavā yugānta sadṛśam rūpam śaila uccalita bandhanam darśayatī muhur muhur kṣatriyāṇām vapurbhiḥ ca tejasā ca balena ca nṛṇām ca rāṣṭraiḥ vistīrṇaiḥ śrāmyati iva vasuṃdharā rāṣṭre rāṣṭre ca bahavaḥ grāmāḥ śata sahasraśas bhūmipānām sahasraiḥ ca teṣām ca balinām balaiḥ grāma ayuta āḍhyaiḥ rāṣṭraiḥ ca bhūmiḥ nirvivarīkṛtā sā iyam nirāmiṣam kṛtvā niśceṣṭam kālam agratas prāptāḥ mama ālayam viṣṇo bhavān ca asyāḥ parā gatiḥ karma bhūmiḥ ihasthānām bhūmiḥ eṣā vyathām gatā yathā na sīdet tat kāryam jagatī eṣā hi śāśvatā asyāḥ hi pīḍane doṣaḥ mahān syāt madhusūdana kriyā lopaḥ ca lokānām dūṣitam ca jagat bhavet śrāmyate vyaktam eva iyam pārthiva ogha prapīḍitā sahajām yā kṣamām tyaktvā cala tvam acalā gatā tat asyāḥ śrutavantaḥ sma tat ca api bhavatā śrutam bhāra avataraṇa artham hi mantrayāmaḥ tvayā saha sat pathe hi sthitāḥ sarve rājānaḥ rāṣṭra vardhanāḥ narāṇām ca trayaḥ varṇāḥ brāhmaṇān anuyāyinaḥ sarvam satya mayam vākyam varṇāḥ dharma pare tathā sarve veda pare viprāḥ sarve vipra pare narāḥ evam jaganti vartante manuṣyāḥ dharma kāraṇāt satām gatiḥ iyam na anyā dharmaḥ ca asyāḥ susādhanam rājñām ca eva vadhaḥ kāryaḥ dharaṇyāḥ bhāra nirṇaye tat āgaccha mahābhāga saha vai mantra kāraṇāt vrajāma meru śikharam puraskṛtya vasuṃdharām uvāca sa jatā maṇḍalam kṛṣṇam bibhrat kṛṣṇa vapūḥ hariḥ sa ca asya urasi vistīrṇe romāñca udgata rājimān śrīvatsaḥ rājate śrīmān stana dvaya mukha āñcitaḥ pīte vasānaḥ vasane lokānām guruḥ avyayaḥ hariḥ saḥ abhavat ālakṣyaḥ sa saṃdhyā abhraḥ iva acalaḥ anujagmuḥ surāḥ sarve tad gata āsakta cakṣuṣaḥ dadṛśuḥ devatāḥ tatra svām sabhām kāmarūpiṇīm meroḥ śikhara vinyastām saṃsaktām sūrya varcasā kāñcana stambha caraṇām vajra saṃghāta toraṇām manaḥ nirmāṇa citra āḍhyām vimāna ākula mālinīm ratna jāla antaravatīm kāmagām ratna bhūṣitām kḷpta ratna samākīrṇām sarva ṛtu kusuma utkaṭām deva māyā dharām divyām nirmitām viśvakarmaṇā tām hṛṣṭa manasaḥ sarve yathāsthānam yathāvayas yathānideśam tridaśāḥ viviśuḥ te sabhām śubhām te niṣeduḥ yathā ukteṣu vimāneṣu āsaneṣu ca bhadrāsaneṣu pīṭheṣu kuthāsu āstaraṇeṣu ca tatas prabhañjanaḥ vāyuḥ brahmanā sādhu coditaḥ mā śabdaḥ iti sarvatra pracakrāma sabhām śubhām babhāṣe dharaṇī vākyam svedāt karuṇa bhāṣiṇī aham ādau purā anena saṃkṣiptā padmayoninā mām ca badhvā kṛtau pūrvam mṛd mayau dvau mahā asurau mahā arṇave prasvapataḥ kāṣṭha kuḍya samau sthitau tau viveśa svayam vāyuḥ brahmaṇā sādhu coditaḥ vāyu prāṇau tu tau gṛhya brahmā parimṛśyan śanais ekam mṛdutaram mene kaṭhinam veda ca aparam tau āgatau samālokya brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ rocayām āsa vasatim guhyām brahmā caturmukhaḥ bahūn varṣa gaṇān apsu śayānau na cakampatuḥ utpapāta āśu śayanāt padmanābhaḥ mahā dyutiḥ tat abhūt tumulam yuddham varṣa saṃkhyāḥ sahasraśas ūcatuḥ prīta manasau devam nārāyaṇam harim saḥ hi āvām yudhi nirjetā tasya āvām vihitau sutau tau ubhau āplutau toye vapurbhyām ekatām gatau medasā tat jalam vyāptam tābhyām antardadhe tadā nārāyaṇaḥ ca bhagavān asṛjat sa punar prajāḥ daityayoḥ medasā channā medinī iti tatas smṛtā prabhāvāt padmanābhasya śāśvatā ca nṛṇām kṛtā varāheṇa punar bhūtvā mārkaṇḍeyasya paśyataḥ viṣāṇena aham ekena toya madhyāt samuddhṛtā hṛtā aham kramatā bhūyas tadā vaḥ agratas baleḥ sakāśāt daityasya viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā sāṃpratam khidyamānā aham enam eva gadādharam anāthā jagataḥ nātham śaraṇyam śaraṇam gatā agniḥ suvarṇasya guruḥ gavām sūryaḥ guruḥ smṛtaḥ akṣatrāṇām guruḥ somaḥ mama nārāyaṇaḥ guruḥ yat aham dhārayāmi ekā jagat sthāvara jaṅgamam mayā dhṛtam dhārayate sarvam etat gadādharaḥ jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa bhāra avataraṇa īpsayā roṣāt tris sapta kṛtvas aham kṣatriyaiḥ viprayojitā sā asmi vedyām samāropya tarpitā nṛpa śoṇitaiḥ bhārgaveṇa pituḥ śrāddhe kaśyapāya niveditā māṃsa medas asthi durgandhā digdhā kṣatriya śoṇitaiḥ sa mām brahmarṣiḥ api āha kim urvi tvam avāṅmukhī sā aham vijñāpitavatī kaśyapam loka bhāvanam sā aham vihīnā vikrāntaiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ śastra vṛttibhiḥ tat mahyam dīyatām bhartā bhagavan tvad samaḥ nṛpaḥ rakṣet sa grāma nagarām yaḥ mām sāgara mālinīm sa śrutvā bhagavān vākyam bāḍham iti abravīt prabhuḥ sā manu prabhavam puṇyam prāpya ikṣvāku kulam mahat vipulena asmi kālena pārthivāt pārthivam gatā bhuktāḥ rāja kulaiḥ ca api mahā ṛṣi kula saṃmitaiḥ bahavaḥ kṣatriyāḥ śūrāḥ mām jitvā divam āśritāḥ te sma kāla vaśam prāpya mayi eva pralayam gatāḥ kṣatriyāṇām balavatām saṃgrāmeṣu anivartinām jagat hita artham kuruta rājñām hetum raṇa kṣaye yadi asti mayi kāruṇyam bhāra śaithilya kāraṇāt aham bhāra saṃtaptā saṃprāptā śaraṇa eṣiṇī bhāraḥ yadi avaroptavyaḥ viṣṇuḥ eṣa bravītu mām uvāca te śrutvā pṛthivī vākyam sarve eva divaukasaḥ bhagavan kriyatām asyāḥ dharaṇyāḥ bhāra saṃnatiḥ śarīra kartā lokānām tvam hi lokasya ca īśvaraḥ yat vā kāryam dhaneśena svayam nārāyaṇena vā yat vā candramasā kāryam bhāskareṇa anilena vā aśvibhyām vā sura agryābhyām sādhyaiḥ vā tridiva ālayaiḥ bṛhaspati uśanobhyām vā kālena kalinā api vā maheśvareṇa vā brahman viśākhena guhena vā yakṣa rākṣasa gandharvaiḥ cāraṇaiḥ vā mahā uragaiḥ gaṅgā mukhābhiḥ divyābhiḥ saridbhiḥ vā sureśvara kṣipram ājñāpaya vibho katham aṃśaḥ prayujyatām yadi te pārthivam kāryam kāryam pārthiva vigrahe katham aṃśāvataraṇam kurmaḥ sarve pitāmaha antarikṣa gatāḥ ye ca pṛthivyām ye ca pārthivāḥ sadasyānām ca viprāṇām pārthivānām kuleṣu ca a yoni jāḥ ca api tanūḥ sṛjāma jagatī tale surāṇām eka kāryāṇām śrutvā etat niścitam mahat devaiḥ parivṛtaḥ prāha vākyam lokapitāmahaḥ rocate me sura śreṣṭhāḥ yuṣmākam api niścayaḥ sṛjadhvam sva śarīra aṃśān tejasā ātma samān bhuvi pārthive bhārate vaṃśe pūrvam eva vijānatā pṛthivyām saṃbhavam imam śrūyatām yat mayā kṛtam samudre aham surāḥ pūrve velām āsādya paścimām sārdham tanūjena kaśyapena mahātmanā kathābhiḥ pūrva vṛttābhiḥ loka veda anugāmibhiḥ iti vṛttaiḥ ca bahubhiḥ purāṇa prabhavaiḥ guṇaiḥ kurvataḥ tu kathāḥ tāḥ tāḥ samudraḥ saha gaṅgayā samīpam ājagāma āśu yuktaḥ toyada mārutaiḥ sa vīci viṣamām kurvan gatim vega taraṃgiṇīm yādaḥ gaṇa vicitreṇa saṃchannaḥ toya vāsasā muktā amala tanuḥ pravāla maṇi bhūṣaṇaḥ yuktaḥ candramasā pūrṇaḥ sa abhra gambhīra nisvanaḥ sa mām paribhavan eva svām velām samatikraman uktaḥ saṃrabdhayā vācā śāntaḥ asi iti tatas mayā śāntaḥ asi iti ukta mātraḥ tu tanu tvam sāgaraḥ gataḥ bhūyas ca eva mayā śaptaḥ samudraḥ saha gaṅgayā sa kāraṇām matim kṛtvā vaḥ hita kāmyayā yasmāt tvam rāja tulyena vapuṣā samupasthitaḥ gaccha arṇava mahīpālaḥ rājā eva tvam bhaviṣyasi tatra api sahajām līlām dhārayan svena tejasā bhaviṣyasi nṛṇām bhartā bhāratānām kula udvahaḥ śāntaḥ asi iti mayā uktaḥ tvam yat ca asi tanutām gataḥ su tanuḥ yaśasā loke śaṃtanuḥ tvam bhaviṣyasi iyam api āyatāpāṅgā gaṅgā sarva aṅga śobhanā rūpiṇī vai sarit śreṣṭhā tatra tvām upayāsyati evam uktaḥ tu mām kruddhaḥ saḥ abhigamya āṛṇavaḥ abravīt mām prabho devadeveśa kimartham śaptavan asi aham tava vidheya ātmā tvad kṛtaḥ tvad parāyaṇaḥ aśapaḥ a sadṛśaiḥ vākyaiḥ ātmajam mām kim ātmanā kṣiptābhiḥ pavanena adbhiḥ spṛṣṭaḥ yadi asi parvaṇi uddhūtaiḥ ca mahā vātaiḥ pravṛddhaiḥ ca balāhakaiḥ parvaṇā ca indu yuktena tribhiḥ kṣubdhaḥ asmi kāraṇaiḥ evam mayi nirālambe śāpāt śithila tām gate kāruṇyam kuru deveśa pramāṇam yadi avekṣase asyāḥ ca deva gaṅgāyāḥ gām gatāyāḥ te ājñayā mad doṣāt sama doṣāyāḥ prasādam kartum arhasi tam aham ślakṣṇayā vācā mahā arṇavam atha abruvam akāraṇa jñam devānām trastam śāpa anila īritam śāpe asmin saritām nātha bhaviṣyam śṛṇu kāraṇam hatsva saritām nātha tyaktvā imām sāgarīm tanum mahodadhe mahīpālaḥ tatra rāja śriyā vṛtaḥ pālayan caturaḥ varṇān raṃsyase salileśvara iyam ca tvām sarit śreṣṭhā bibhratī mānuṣīm tanum tat kāla ramaṇīya aṅgā gaṅgā paricariṣyati anayā saha jāhnavyā modamānaḥ mama ājñayā prājāpatyena vidhinā gaṅgayā saha sāgara vasavaḥ pracyutāḥ svargāt praviṣṭāḥ ca rasātalam teṣām utpādana arthāya tvam mayā viniyojitaḥ tān jāhnavī garbhān apatya artham dadāmi aham vibhāvasoḥ tulya guṇān surāṇām prīti vardhanān utpādya tvam vasūn śīghram kṛtvā kuru kulam mahat praveṣṭāsi tanum tyaktvā punar sāgara sāgarīm evam etat mayā pūrvam hita artham vaḥ sura uttamāḥ bhaviṣyam paśyatā bhāram pṛthivyāḥ pārthiva ātmakam tat eṣa śaṃtanoḥ vaṃśaḥ pṛthivyām ropitaḥ mayā vasavaḥ yatra gaṅgāyām utpannāḥ tridivaukasaḥ adya api bhuvi gāṅgeyaḥ tatra eva vasuḥ aṣṭamaḥ dvitīyāyām striyām sṛṣṭā dvitīyā śaṃtanoḥ tanuḥ vicitravīryaḥ dyutimān āsīt rājā pratāpavān pāṇḍuḥ ca dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ ca vikhyātau puruṣa ṛṣabhau tatra pāṇḍoḥ śriyā juṣṭe dve bhārye yauvana sthite dhṛtarāṣṭrasya rājñaḥ tu bhāryā ekā tulya cāriṇī atra vaḥ aṃśāḥ vibhajyantām vipakṣaḥ pakṣaḥ eva ca putrāṇām hi tayoḥ rājñoḥ bhavitā vigrahaḥ mahān teṣām vimarde dāyādye nṛpāṇām bhavitā kṣayaḥ iṣyati dvāparasya yugasya ante mayā dṛṣṭam purātane kṣayam yāsyanti śastreṇa pārthivāḥ saha vāhanaiḥ tatra avaśiṣṭān manujān suptān niśi vicetasaḥ dhakṣyate śaṃkarasya aṃśaḥ pāvakena astra tejasā samāptam idam ākhyāsye tṛtīyam dvāparam yugam maheśvara aṃśe apasṛte tatas māheśvaram yugam tiṣyam prapatsyate paścāt yugam dāruṇa mānuṣam maheśvaram kumāram ca dvau ca devau samāśritāḥ bhaviṣyanti narāḥ sarve loke na sthavira āyuṣaḥ tat eṣa nirṇayaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ pṛthivyām pārthiva antakaḥ aṃśāvataraṇam sarve surāḥ kuruta māciram dharmasya aṃśaḥ atha kuntyām vai mādryām ca viniyujyatām vigrahasya kaliḥ mūlam gāndhāryām viniyujyatām etau pakṣau bhaviṣyanti rājānaḥ kāla coditāḥ jāta rāgāḥ pṛthivī arthe sarve saṃgrāma lālasāḥ gacchatu iyam vasumatī svām yonim loka dhāriṇī sṛṣṭaḥ ayam naiṣṭhikaḥ rājñām upāyaḥ loka viśrutaḥ śrutvā pitāmaha vacaḥ sā jagāma yathāgatam pṛthivī saha kālena vadhāya pṛthivīkṣitām naram ca eva purāṇa ṛṣim śeṣam ca dharaṇīdharam sanatkumāram sādhyān ca devān ca agni purogamān varuṇam ca yamam ca eva sūryācandramasau tathā gandharva apsarasaḥ ca eva rudra ādityān tathā aśvinaḥ tatas aṃśān avanim devāḥ sarve eva avatārayan yathā te kathitam pūrvam aṃśāvataraṇam mayā ayoni jāḥ yoni jāḥ ca te devāḥ pṛthivī tale daitya dānava
