sarvaśas siṃha ṛṣabha mṛgaiḥ nāgaiḥ vāji sārasa barhiṇaiḥ bhāsvanti tāni dṛśyante vimānāni sahasraśas ete rudrāḥ tathā ādityāḥ vasavaḥ atha aśvinaḥ api sādhyāḥ devāḥ tathā anye ca api avandan tān yathākramam aho vai mahat āścaryam vāsudevasya saṃśrayāt tatas candana cūrṇaiḥ ca puṣpa varṣaiḥ ca sarvaśas kiranti paurāḥ sarvān tān pūjayantaḥ divaukasaḥ lājaiḥ praṇāmaiḥ dhūpaiḥ ca vāc buddhi niyatāḥ tathā dvārakā vāsinaḥ sarve pūjayanti divaukasaḥ sātyakim ca ulmukam ca eva vipṛthum ca mahā balam etān pariṣvajya tadā mūrdhani ca āghrāya vīryavān andhakam ca śubha akṣam ca tatas vacanam abravīt vāsavaḥ sātvatān sarvān eṣa vaḥ yadu nandanaḥ yojayitvā raṇe ca eva yaśasā pauruṣeṇa ca eṣa bāṇam raṇe jitvā dvārakām punar āgatāḥ sahasrabāhoḥ bāhūnām kṛtvā kṣayam anuttamam sthāpayitvā dvi bāhu tve prāptaḥ ayam sva purīm hariḥ tat api avasitam kṛtsnam naṣṭa śokāḥ vayam kṛtāḥ pibantaḥ madhu mādhvīkam raṃsyāmaḥ prīti saṃyutāḥ kālaḥ yāsyati aviratam viṣayeṣu eva sajja tām bāhūnām saṃśrayāt sarve vayam asya mahātmanaḥ pranaṣṭa śokāḥ raṃsyāmaḥ sarve eva amarāḥ sukham evam uktvā pariṣvajya kṛṣṇam kamala locanam puraṃdaraḥ divam yātaḥ sarva amara gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ dvārakām prāpya kṛṣṇaḥ tu reme yadu gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ evam eṣaḥ vai pṛthivyām pṛthivīpate etaiḥ ca kāraṇaiḥ śrīmān vasudeva kule prabhuḥ jātaḥ vṛṣṇiṣu devakyām yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi nivṛtte nārada praśne mayā uktam te samāsatas viṣṇoḥ tu māthure kalpe yatra te saṃśayaḥ mahān vāsudeva gatiḥ ca eva sā mayā samudāhṛtā āścaryaḥ ca eva na anyaḥ asti kṛṣṇaḥ ca āścarya saṃnidhiḥ sarveṣu āścarya kalpeṣu na asti āścaryam avaiṣṇavam eṣa dhātā vidhātā ca saṃhartā kālaḥ eva ca iti uktam bāṇa yuddham te māhātmyam keśavasya ca vaṃśa pratiṣṭhām atulām śravaṇāt eva lapsyase keśavasya ca māhātmyam na adharmaḥ tān bhajiṣyati eṣā te vaiṣṇavā caryā mayā kārtsnyena kīrtitā āścarya parvam akhilam yaḥ hi idam dhārayet nṛpa na aśubham prāpnuyāt kiṃcid dīrgham āyuḥ avāpnuyāt uvāca iti pārikṣitaḥ rājā vaiśaṃpāyana bhāṣitam śrutavan amalaḥ bhūtvā hari vaṃśam dvijarṣabhāḥ evam śaunaka saṃkṣepāt vistareṇa tathā eva ca proktāḥ vai sarva vaṃśāḥ te kim bhūyas kathayāmi te uvāca kasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ vaṃśaḥ pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām uvāca pārikṣitasya kāśyāyām dvau putrau saṃbabhūvatuḥ candrāpīḍaḥ ca nṛpatiḥ sūryāpīḍaḥ ca mokṣa vid candrāpīḍasya putrāṇām śatam uttama dhanvinām teṣām jyeṣṭhaḥ tu rājā āsīt pure vāraṇasāhvaye satya karṇaḥ mahā bāhuḥ yajvā vipula dakṣiṇaḥ satyakarṇasya dāyādaḥ śvetakarṇaḥ pratāpavān sucāroḥ duhitā subhrūḥ mālinī bhrātṛ mālini sā dṛṣṭvā saṃprayātam tam mālinī pṛṣṭhatas anvagāt tam a pāśya ca tatra eva rājānam sā anvagacchata pativratā mahābhāgā draupadī iva purā patīn dayā artham tasya meghāḥ tu prādurāsan mahātmanaḥ śraviṣṭhāyāḥ ca putrau dvau paippalādau ca tau dvijau dṛṣṭvā kṛpā anvitau gṛhya tam prakṣālayatām jale aja śyāmau ca pārśvau tau ubhau api samāhitau tathā eva ca samārūḍhau ajapārśvaḥ tatas abhavat sa tu vemaka śālāyām ubhābhyām abhivardhitaḥ teṣām putrāḥ ca pautrāḥ ca yugapad tulya jīvinaḥ saḥ eṣa pauravaḥ vaṃśaḥ pāṇḍavānām pratiṣṭhitaḥ ślokaḥ api ca atra gītaḥ ayam nāhuṣeṇa yayātinā acandra arka grahā bhūmiḥ bhavet api na saṃśayaḥ uvāca uktaḥ ayam harivaṃśaḥ te parvāṇi nikhilāni ca yathā purā uktāni tathā vyāsa śiṣyeṇa dhīmatā prīṇāti asmān amṛta vat sarva pāpa praṇāśanam uvāca tasmin satre samāpte tu rājā pārikṣitaḥ tadā yaṣṭum sa vājimedhena saṃbhārān upacakrame bhū ṛtvij purohita ācāryān āhūya idam uvāca ha tatas asya vijñāya cikīrṣitam tadā kṛṣṇaḥ mahātmā sahasā ājagāma pārikṣitam draṣṭum adīna sattvam dvaipāyanaḥ sarva parāvara jñaḥ pārikṣitaḥ tu nṛpatiḥ dṛṣṭvā tam ṛṣim āgatam arghya pādya āsanam dattvā pūjayāmāsa śāstrāt tau ca upaviṣṭau abhitas sadasyāḥ tasya śaunaka kathāḥ bahuvidhāḥ citrāḥ cakrāte veda saṃhitāḥ tatas kathā ante nṛpatiḥ codayāmāsa tam munim pitāmaham pāṇḍavānām ātmanaḥ prapitāmaham tvayā tu abhihitam brahman śaṅkhe kṣīram iva āhitam na amṛtena api tṛptiḥ syāt yathā svarga sukhena vā tathā tṛptim na gacchāmi śrutvā imām bhāratīm kathām hetuḥ kurūṇām nāśasya rājasūyaḥ mataḥ mama duḥsahānām yathā dhvaṃsaḥ rājanyānām upaplavaḥ rājasūyaḥ hi somena śrūyate pūrvam āhṛtaḥ āhṛtaḥ varuṇena api tasya ante su mahā kratoḥ tatra api āḍībakam abhūt yuddham kṣatra vināśanam tatas anantaram āryeṇa pāṇḍavena api dustaraḥ mahābhārata saṃhāraḥ saṃbhṛtaḥ agniḥ iva kratuḥ rājasūyaḥ mahā yajñaḥ kimartham na nivāritaḥ rājasūye hi asaṃhārye yajña aṅgaiḥ ca durāsadaiḥ mithyā praṇīte yajña aṅge prajānām saṃkṣayaḥ dhruvaḥ bhavān api ca sarveṣām pūrveṣām naḥ pitāmahaḥ atīta anāgata jñaḥ ca nāthaḥ ca ādi karaḥ ca naḥ anāthāḥ hi aparādhyante ku netāraḥ ca mānavāḥ uvāca kālena adya parītāḥ te tava vatsa pitāmahāḥ na mām bhaviṣyam papracchuḥ na ca apṛṣṭaḥ bravīmi aham parihartum na śakṣyāmi kāla niṣṭhām hi tām gatim tvayā tu idam aham pṛṣṭaḥ vakṣyāmi āgantu bhāvi yat atas ca balavān kālaḥ śrutvā api na kariṣyasi aśvamedhaḥ kratuḥ śreṣṭhaḥ kṣatriyāṇām pariśrutaḥ tena bhāvena te yajñam vāsavaḥ dharṣayiṣyati daivam puruṣakāreṇa mā yajethāḥ ca tam kratum na ca aparādhaḥ śakrasya na upadhyāya gaṇasya te yathā yaṣṭā nṛpaḥ svargam gamiṣyati yuga kṣaye tathā yajña phalānām ca vikretāraḥ dvijātayaḥ uvāca tvayā dhṛtaḥ kratuḥ ca eva vājimedhaḥ paraṃtapa kṣatriyāḥ na āhariṣyanti yāvat bhūmiḥ dhariṣyati nivṛttau aśvamedhasya vipra śāpa agni tejasā mama nimittam iti ced bhayam tīvram ca jāyate katham hi akīrtyā saṃyuktaḥ sukṛtī madvidhaḥ janaḥ lokān utsahate gantum kham sa pāśaḥ iva dvijaḥ yathā hi anāgatam idam dṛṣṭam atra praṇāśanam yajñasya punarāvṛttiḥ yadi asti āśvāsayasva mām uvāca tejasā abhyāhṛtam tejaḥ tejasi eva avatiṣṭhate audbhidaḥ bhavitā kaścid senā nīḥ kāśyapaḥ dvijaḥ māhariṣyati rāja indra śveta graham iva antakaḥ yathābalam manuṣyāṇām kartṝṇām dāsyate phalam yugānta dvāram ṛṣibhiḥ saṃvṛtam vicariṣyati tadā prabhṛti hāsyante nṛṇām prāṇāḥ purā ākṛtīḥ tadā sūkṣmaḥ mahā udarkaḥ dustaraḥ dāna mūlavān cāturāśramya śithilaḥ dharmaḥ pravicaliṣyati tadā hi alpena tapasā siddhim yāsyanti mānavāḥ āsannam viprakṛṣṭam vā yadi kālam na vidmahe tasmāt dvāpara vidhvaṃsāt yuga antam spṛhayāmi aham prāptāḥ vayam hi tam kālam anayā dharma tṛṣṇayā prāptāḥ vayam ca dharmam svam sukham alpena karmaṇā uvāca yuga ante pūrvarūpāṇi bhagavān abravīt tadā uvāca hartāraḥ bali bhāgasya pārthivāḥ prabhaviṣyanti a kṣatriyāḥ ca rājānaḥ viprāḥ śūdra upajīvinaḥ śūdrāḥ ca brāhmaṇa ācārāḥ bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye kāṇḍapṛṣṭhāḥ śrotriyāḥ ca havīṃṣi bharata ṛṣabha śilpavantaḥ anṛta pare narāḥ madya āmiṣa priyāḥ rāja vṛtte sthitāḥ corāḥ cora śīlinaḥ bhṛtyāḥ anirviṣṭa bhujaḥ bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye dhanāni ślāghanīyāni satām vṛttam apūjitam pranaṣṭa cetanāḥ martyāḥ mukta keśāḥ vicūlinaḥ una ṣoḍaśa varṣāḥ ca narāḥ tadā aṭṭa śūlāḥ janapadāḥ śiva śūlāḥ catuṣpathāḥ pramadāḥ keśa śūlāḥ ca bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye śūdrāḥ bho vādinaḥ ca eva bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye tapaḥ yajña artha vedānām vikretāraḥ dvijātayaḥ ṛtavaḥ ca bhaviṣyanti viparītāḥ yuga kṣaye śukla danta ajita akṣāḥ ca muṇḍāḥ kāṣāya vāsasaḥ śūdrāḥ dharmam cariṣyanti śākya buddha upajīvinaḥ śvāpada pracura tvam ca gavām ca eva parikṣayaḥ svādūnām vinivṛttiḥ ca vidyāt anta gate yuge antyāḥ madhye nivatsyanti madhyāḥ ca antāvasāyinaḥ yathānimnam prajāḥ sarvāḥ gamiṣyanti yuga kṣaye tathā dvi hāyanāḥ damyāḥ tathā palvala karṣakāḥ citra varṣī ca parjanyaḥ yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati mūṣara abahulā bhūmiḥ panthānaḥ nagara antarā pitṛ kṛtyāni deyāni vidhamantaḥ sutāḥ tadā haraṇāya prapatsyante lobha anṛta virodhitāḥ bhaviṣyanti yugasya ante nāryaḥ keśaiḥ alaṃkṛtāḥ yuga ante samanuprāpte na anyā bhāryā samā ratiḥ kuśīla anārya bhūyiṣṭham vṛthak rūpa samāvṛtam puruṣa alpam bahu strīkam tat yugāntasya lakṣaṇam rāja cora ādi daṇḍa ārtaḥ janaḥ kṣayam upaiṣyati sasya niṣpattiḥ aphalā taruṇāḥ vṛddha śīlinaḥ varṣāsu vātāḥ puruṣāḥ nīcāḥ śarkara varṣiṇaḥ vaiśya ācārāḥ ca rājanyāḥ dhana dhānya upajīvinaḥ bhaviṣyanti apravṛttāḥ prapatsyante samayāḥ śapathāḥ tathā ṛṇam ca vinaya bhraṃśaḥ yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati bhaviṣyati aphalaḥ harṣaḥ krodhaḥ ca sa phalaḥ nṛṇām a śāstra vihitā prajñā evam eva bhaviṣyati sarvaḥ sarvam vijānāti vṛddhān an upasevya ca na kṣatrāṇi niyokṣyanti vikarma sthāḥ dvijātayaḥ cora prāyāḥ ca rājānaḥ yugānte pratyupasthite kuṇḍāḥ vṛṣāḥ naikṛtikāḥ surā pāḥ brahma vādinaḥ a yājyān yājayiṣyanti tathā abhakṣyasya bhakṣiṇaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ dhana tṛṣṇā ārtāḥ yugānte samupasthite eka śaṅkhāḥ tathā nāryaḥ gavedhu kapinaddhakāḥ nakṣatrāṇi vihīnāni viparītāḥ diśaḥ tathā pitṝn putrāḥ niyokṣyanti vadhvaḥ śvaśrūḥ ca karmasu a kṛta agrāṇi bhokṣyanti narāḥ ca eva agnihotriṇaḥ bhikṣām balim a dattvā ca bhokṣyanti puruṣāḥ svayam patīn suptān vañcayitvā gamiṣyanti striyaḥ aṇyataḥ puruṣāḥ ca prasuptāsu bhāryāsu ca para striyam na kṛta pratikartā ca kāle kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati vilulite loke manuṣyāḥ kena pālitāḥ nivatsyanti kimācārāḥ kimāhāra vihāriṇaḥ kiṃkarmāṇaḥ kim īhantaḥ kiṃpramāṇāḥ kim āyuṣaḥ kām ca kāṣṭhām samāsādya prapatsyanti kṛtam yugam uvāca atas ūrdhvam cyute dharme guṇa hīnāḥ prajāḥ tatas śīla vyasanam āsādya prāpsyante hrāsam āyuṣaḥ āyuḥ hārnyāḥ bala glāniḥ bala glānyāḥ vivarṇa tā vaivarṇyāt vyādhi saṃpīḍā nirvedaḥ vyādhi pīḍanāt nirvedāt ātma saṃbodhaḥ saṃbodhāt dharma śīla tā evam gatvā parām kāṣṭhām prapatsyanti kṛtam yugam uddeśataḥ dharma śīlāḥ kecid madhyastha tām gatāḥ vimarśa śīlāḥ kecid tu hetuvāda kutūhalāḥ pratyakṣam anumānam ca pramāṇam iti niścitāḥ pramāṇam kim kariṣyati na iti paṇḍita māninaḥ apramāṇam kariṣyanti veda uktam apare janāḥ nāstikya paramāḥ ca api kecid dharma vilopakāḥ bhaviṣyanti narāḥ mūḍhāḥ mandāḥ paṇḍita māninaḥ tadātva mātra śraddheyāḥ śāstra jñāna vimūrchitāḥ dāmbhikāḥ te bhaviṣyanti vāda śīla parāyaṇāḥ tadā vicalite dharme janāḥ śeṣa puraskṛtāḥ śubhāni eva ācariṣyanti dāna satya samanvitāḥ bhaviṣyati tadā lokaḥ tat kaṣāyasya lakṣaṇam viprāṇām śāśvatām vṛttim yadā varṇa avaraḥ janaḥ kaṣāya upaplave kāle jñāna vidyā praṇāśane mahā yuddham mahā nādam mahā varṣam mahā bhayam bhaviṣyati yuge kṣīṇe tat kaṣāyasya lakṣaṇam vipra rūpāṇi rakṣāṃsi rājānaḥ karṇa vedinaḥ niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkārāḥ munayaḥ ca abhimāninaḥ kravyādāḥ brahma rūpeṇa sarva bhakṣāḥ vṛthāvratāḥ mūrkhāḥ sva artha pare lubdhāḥ kṣudrāḥ kṣudra paricchadāḥ vyavāhāra upavṛttāḥ ca cyutāḥ dharmāt ca śāśvatāt hartāraḥ para ratnānām para dāra pradharṣakāḥ kāma ātmānaḥ durātmānaḥ sa upadhāḥ priya sāhasāḥ teṣu prabhavamāneṣu tulya śīleṣu sarvatas utpannāḥ ye kṛta yuge pradhāna puruṣa āśrayāḥ kathā yogena tān sarvān pūjayiṣyanti mānavāḥ sasya corāḥ bhaviṣyanti tathā caila apahāriṇaḥ bhakṣya bhojya harāḥ ca eva bhāṇḍānām ca eva hāriṇaḥ corāḥ cora kṣaye ca api kṛte kṣemam bhaviṣyati narāḥ śrayiṣyanti vanam kara bhāra prapīḍitāḥ yajña karmaṇi uparate rakṣāṃsi śvāpadāni ca koṭi mūṣaka sarpāḥ ca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān kṣemam subhikṣam ārogyam sāmagryam atha bandhubhiḥ uddeśena nara śreṣṭha bhaviṣyanti yuga kṣaye svayam pālāḥ svayam corāḥ yuga saṃbhāra saṃbhṛtāḥ maṇḍalaiḥ prabhaviṣyanti deśe deśe pṛthak pṛthak sva deśebhyaḥ paribhraṣṭāḥ niḥsārāḥ saha bandhubhiḥ narāḥ tadā bhaviṣyanti sarve kāla pratīkṣiṇaḥ tadā skandhe samādāya kumārān pradrutā bhayāt kauśikīm saṃśrayiṣyanti narāḥ kṣudh bhaya pīḍitāḥ aṅgān vaṅgān kaliṅgān ca kāśmīrān atha mekalān ṛṣikānta giri droṇīḥ saṃśrayiṣyanti mānavāḥ kṛtsnam ca himavat pārśvam kūlam ca lavaṇāmbhasaḥ na eva śūnyā na ca a śūnyā bhaviṣyati vasuṃdharā goptāraḥ ca api a goptāraḥ prabhaviṣyanti śāsinaḥ mṛgaiḥ matsyaiḥ vihaṃgaiḥ ca śvāpadaiḥ sarva kīṭakaiḥ madhu śāka phalaiḥ mūlaiḥ vartayiṣyanti mānavāḥ cīram parṇam ca vividham valkalāni ajināni ca bījānām ākṛtim nimneṣu īhante kāṣṭha śaṅkubhiḥ yatnatas nadī srotāṃsi rotsyanti toya artham kūlam āśritāḥ tanūruhaiḥ yathā jātaiḥ sa mala antara saṃvṛtaiḥ bahu apatyāḥ prajā hīnāḥ krūrāḥ lakṣaṇa varjitāḥ evam bhaviṣyanti tadā manuṣyāḥ kāla kāritāḥ hīnāt hīnam tadā dharmam prajā samanuvartsyati āyuḥ tatra ca martyānām param triṃśat bhaviṣyati durbalāḥ viṣaya glānāḥ rajasā samabhiplutāḥ bhaviṣyati tadā teṣām rogaiḥ indriya saṃkṣayaḥ āyuḥ prakṣaya saṃrodhāt hiṃsā ca uparamiṣyati śuśrūṣavaḥ bhaviṣyanti sādhūnām darśane ratāḥ satyam ca api prapatsyanti vyavahāra apaśaṅkayā bhaviṣyanti ca kāmānām alābhāt dharma śīlinaḥ kariṣyanti ca saṃkocam sva pakṣa kṣaya pīḍitāḥ evam śuśrūṣavaḥ dāne satye prāṇa abhirakṣaṇe catuṣpāda pravṛttam ca dharmam āpsyanti mānavāḥ dharma abhimānānām guṇeṣu parivartatām yathā hāniḥ krama prāptā tathā vṛddhiḥ krama āgatā sādhu vṛttiḥ kṛta yuge kaṣāye hāniḥ ucyate ekaḥ eva tu kālaḥ saḥ hīna varṇaḥ yathā śaśī pūrṇaḥ ca tapasā hīnaḥ yathā kali yuge tathā a nirṇiktam a vijñātam dāyādyam iva dhāryate yaj dānam tapaḥ nāma brahmacaryam su pūjitam guṇaiḥ karma abhinirvṛttiḥ guṇāḥ tathyena karmaṇā puruṣam dṛṣṭvā deśa kāla anuvartinī yuge yuge yathākālam ṛṣibhiḥ samudāhṛtā iha dharma artha kāmānām vedānām ca pratikriyā ca śubhāḥ puṇyāḥ tathā eva āyuḥ yuge yuge yathā yugānām parivartanāni cira pravṛttāni vidhi svabhāvāt māna lokaḥ kṣaya udayābhyām parivartamānaḥ uvāca iti evam āśvāsayataḥ rājānam janamejayam atīta anāgatam vākyam ṛṣeḥ pariṣadā śrutam amṛtasya iva ca āsvādaḥ prabhā candramasaḥ yathā dharma artha kāma saṃyuktam karuṇam vīra harṣaṇam ramaṇīyam tat ākhyānam kṛtsnam pariṣadā śrutam kecid aśrūṇi mumucuḥ śrutvā dadhyuḥ tathā apare itihāsam tam ṛṣiṇā pārāśaryeṇa darśitam sadasya antar abhyanujñāya kṛtvā ca api pradakṣiṇam punar drakṣyāmaḥ iti uktvā jagāma bhagavān ṛṣiḥ loke pravadatām śreṣṭham śiṣṭāḥ sarve tapodhanāḥ yāte bhagavati vyāse viprāḥ saha mahā ṛṣibhiḥ pannagānām su ghorāṇām kṛtvā tām vaira yātanām jagāma roṣam utsṛtya rājā viṣam iva uragaḥ hotra agni dīpta śirasam paritrāya ca takṣakam āstīkaḥ api āśrama padam jagāma ca mahā muniḥ rājā api hāstinapuram praviveśa jana āvṛtaḥ anvaśāsat ca muditaḥ tadā pramuditāḥ prajāḥ dīkṣitaḥ vājimedhāya vidhivat bhūri dakṣiṇaḥ saṃjñaptam aśvam tatra asya devī kāśyā vapuṣṭamā saṃviveśa upagamya atha vidhi dṛṣṭena karmaṇā tām tu sarva anavadya aṅgām cakame vāsavaḥ tadā saṃjñaptam aśvam āviśya tayā miśrībabhūva saḥ kathayāmāsa rājarṣeḥ śaśāpa saḥ puraṃdaram yadi asti me yajña phalam tapaḥ vā rakṣataḥ prajāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vājimedhena na yakṣyanti iti śaunaka ṛtvijaḥ ca abravīt kruddhaḥ sa rājā janamejayaḥ iti uktāḥ tatyajuḥ viprāḥ tam nṛpam jāta manyavaḥ amarṣāt anvaśāsat ca patnīśālā gatāḥ striyaḥ asatīm vapuṣṭamām etām nirvāsayata me gṛhāt śauṇḍīryam me anayā bhagnam yaśaḥ mānaḥ ca dūṣitaḥ na enām draṣṭum api icchāmi parikliṣṭām iva srajam na svādu saḥ aśnāti naraḥ sukham svapiti vā rahaḥ anvāste yaḥ priyām bhāryām pareṇa mṛditām iha evam uccais prabhāṣantam kruddham pārikṣitam nṛpam gandharva rājaḥ provāca viśvāvasuḥ idam vācaḥ tri yajña śata yajvānam vāsavaḥ tvām na mṛṣyati na duṣyati iyam patnī te vihitā iyam vapuṣṭamā Rambhā nāma apsarāḥ devī kāśi rāja sutā matā sā eṣā yoṣit varā rājan ratna bhūtā anubhūyatām yajvā hi asi kuru śreṣṭha samṛddhyā vāsava upamaḥ māyā eṣā vāsavena iha prayuktā vighnam icchatā yajñe vivaram āsādya saṃjñaptam dṛśya vājinam ratim indreṇa rambhāyām manyase yām vapuṣṭamām atha te guravaḥ śaptāḥ tri yajña śata yājinaḥ bhraṃśitaḥ tvam ca viprāḥ ca phalāt indra samāt iha tvattaḥ ca eva su durdharṣāt tri yajña śata yājinaḥ ekena vai tat ubhayam tīrṇam śakreṇa māyayā saḥ eṣa su mahā tejāḥ vijigīṣuḥ puraṃdaraḥ mā vāsavam mā ca gurum ātmāṇam mā vapuṣtamām aiśvaryeṇa aśvam āviśya deva indreṇa abhiroṣitaḥ strī ratnam upabhuṅkṣva imām apāpām vigata jvaraḥ apāpāḥ tyajyamānāḥ vai śapeyuḥ api yoṣitaḥ aduṣṭāḥ tu striyaḥ rājan divyāḥ tu sa viśeṣataḥ bhānoḥ prabhā śikhā vahneḥ vedī hotre tathā āhutiḥ parāmṛṣṭā api a saṃraktā na upaduṣyanti yoṣitaḥ grāhyāḥ lālayitavyāḥ ca pūjyāḥ ca satatam budhaiḥ śīlavatyaḥ namaskāryāḥ pūjyāḥ striyaḥ iva striyaḥ uvāca evam sa viśvāvasunā anunītaḥ prasādam āgamya vapuṣṭamāyām cakāra mithyā vyatiśaṅkita ātmā śāntim parām tatra sa dharma juṣṭām ramayan idam mahākāvyam ṛṣeḥ mahātmanaḥ paṭhan nṛṇām pūjyatamaḥ bhavet naraḥ mucyati kalmaṣāt naraḥ yathā hi puṣpa prabhavam phalam drumāt tatas prajāyanti punar ca pādapāḥ tathā mahā ṛṣi prabhavāḥ imāḥ giraḥ pravardhayante tam ṛṣim pravartitāḥ na ca āpnoti ciram ca bandhanam ca labhate vipulam api dhanam labhet ca vaiśyaḥ sugatim iyāt śravaṇāt ca śūdra jātiḥ purāṇam etat caritam mahātmanām adhītya buddhim labhate ca naiṣṭhikīm vihāya duḥkhāni vimukta saṅgaḥ sa vīta rāgaḥ vicaret vasuṃdharām iti etat ākhyānam udāhṛtam vaḥ pratismarantaḥ dvija maṇḍaleṣu iti caritam idam mahātmanām ṛṣi kṛtam adbhuta vīrya karmaṇām
